本文件按照 GB/T 1.1 一 202 久标准化工作导则第工部分:标准化文件的结构和起草规则的规定起惠。	This document begins in accordance with the provisions of Part 1 of the GB/T 1.1 202-long Standardization Work Guidelines: Structure and drafting rules for standardization documents.	yes
本文件代替 GB 18030 一 2005 信息技术 ”中文编码字符集与 GB 18030 一 2005 相比,除结构调整和编辑性改动外,主要扩术变化如下:	This document replaces the GB 18030 I 2005 Information Technology” Chinese coding character set compared with GB 18030 I 2005. Apart from structural adjustments and editorial changes, the main expansion changes are as follows:	yes
增加了本文件适用对象(见第 1 章)，	The target audience for this document has been added (see Chapter 1),	yes
在双字节编码区更改了 10 个竖排标点和8 个汉字构件所对应的 GB/I 13000 代码位置,并其除了 6 个重复编码的汉字构件和 9 个重复编码的汉字( 见附录 D,2005 年版的附录A)，	The GB/I 13000 code positions corresponding to the 10 vertical punctuation points and 8 Chinese character components have been changed in the double-byte coding area, and in addition to the 6 repeatedly coded kanji components and 9 repeatedly coded Chinese characters (see Appendix D, Appendix A of the 2005 edition),	yes
在四字节编码区更改了18 个 GB/T 13000 代码位置(见附录 D,2005 年版的附录D);	18 GB/T 13000 code locations were changed in the four-byte coding area (see Appendix D, Appendix D of the 2005 edition);	yes
删除了附录 ”追加的汉字及部首/部件 “ 见 2005 年版的附录 〇 ，	Removed the appendix “Additional Chinese characters and headings/parts” see Appendix 0 of the 2005 edition,	yes
增加了实现的级别 " (见第9草);	The level of achievement was added” (see draft 9);	yes

GB 18030 一 2022	GB 18030 I 2022	yes
信息扩术 ”中文编码字符集	Information Expansion” Chinese Coding Character Set	yes
1 本文件规定了信息技术用的中文图形字符及甚二进制编码的十六进制表示 。	1 This document specifies the hexadecimal representation of Chinese graphic characters and very binary coding used in information technology.	yes
本文件适用于中文和其他文字图形字符信息的处理、交换、存储、传给、显现 、输入和输出。	This document applies to the processing, exchange, storage, transmission, display, input, and output of Chinese and other text and graphic character information.	no
本文件适用于为具备中文和其他文字图形字符信息化处理及交换功能的技术类产品,包括但不限于以输入法、光学字符识别 (OCR)、编辑 校对、机融翻诺、语音合成、文字转写、乔能写作等为代表的软件产品 , 以及以计算机、通信终端设备、电子书阅读毅、学习机等为代表的便件产品 。	This document applies to technical products with informatization processing and exchange functions for Chinese and other text and graphic characters, including but not limited to software products represented by input methods, optical character recognition (OCR), editing and proofreading, machine translation, speech synthesis, text transcription, Qiaoneng writing, etc., as well as stationery products represented by computers, communication terminal equipment, e-book reading tools, learning machines, etc.	no

下列文件中的内容通过文中的规范性引用而构成本文件必不可少的条款。	The content in the following documents forms the essential provisions of this document through normative references in the text.	no
其中, 注日期的引用文件,仅该日期对应的版本适用于本文件;不注日期的引用文件,其最新厂本(包括所有的修改单)适用于本文件。	Among them, for dated reference files, only the version corresponding to that date applies to this document; for undated reference files, the latest version (including all revisions) applies to this document.	no

4 字汇	4 vocabulary	no
4.1 概述	4.1 Overview	no
本文件收录的字符以单字节、双字或四字节编码 。	The characters included in this file are single-byte, double-word, or four-byte encodings.	no
单字节部分收录了 GB/T 11383 一 1989 的 0x00~0x7F 全部 128 个字符 。	The single-byte section contains all 128 characters of 0x00~0x7F from GB/T 11383 1989.	no
4.3 双字节部分	4.3 Double byte portion	no
双字节部分收录了 GB/T 2312 一 1980 中的全部图形字符 GB/T 13000 中的CJK 统一汉字以及部分图形字符。	The double-byte section includes all of the graphic characters in GB/T 2312 and 1980, the CJK unified Chinese characters from GB/T 13000, as well as some graphic characters.	no
双字节部分的字符按照附录 A 的规定。	The characters for the double-byte portion are as specified in Appendix A.	no
其中,表意文字描述符的图形、代码位置和功能应符合附录 B 的规定 。	Among them, the graphics, code location, and function of the ideographic descriptor shall meet the requirements of Appendix B.	no
注: GB/T 13000 对中国、日本、恩国、越南等国家和地区使用的汉字统一编码。	Note: GB/T 13000 is a unified code for Chinese characters used in countries and regions such as China, Japan, Nguk, Vietnam, etc.	no
具备独有抽象字形的汉字,赋予单独的代码位置;来源不同而抽象字形相同的汉字, 则赋予共用的代码位置。	Chinese characters with unique abstract glyphs are given a separate code location; Chinese characters with different sources and the same abstract glyph are given a shared code location.	no
经过编码的汉字称为CJK 统一汉字 CCJK Unified Ideographs,其中 CJK 表示中国、日本、韩国。	The coded kanji is called the CJK unified Chinese character CCJK Unified Ideographs, where CJK represents China, Japan, and Korea.	no
4.4 四字节部分	4.4 four-byte portion	no
四字节部分收录了上述双字节字符之外的 GB/T 13000 中的 66 个CJK统一汉字(9FA6 一 9FEF，不包括 9FB4~9FBB 的8个字符)、CJK 统一汉字扩充 A、CJK 统一汉字扩充 BCJK 统一汉字扩充 C、 CJK 统一汉字扩充 DCJK 统一汉字扩充下 .CJK 统一汉字扩充 F 和已经 在 GB/ 工 13000 中编码的少数民族文字的字符。	The four-byte section includes 66 CJK unified Chinese characters (9FA6 one 9FEF, not including the 8 characters from 9FB4 to 9FBB) in GB/T 13000 other than the double-byte characters described above, CJK unified Chinese characters expanded A, CJK unified Chinese characters expanded BCJK unified kanji expanded C, CJK unified kanji expanded DCJK unified kanji expanded C, CJK unified kanji expanded DCJK unified kanji under DCJK unified kanji expansion F and characters already coded in GB/G13000.	no
四字节部分的字符按照附录 C 的规定 。	The characters in the four-byte part are specified in Appendix C.	no
5 总体结构	5 Overall structure	no
正文中凡数字前标有 0x 的表示采用十六进制,未标有 0x 的表示采用十进制。	In the main text, any representation marked with 0x before a number is in hexadecimal, and anything not marked with 0x is in decimal.	no
附录中凡编码的表示均采用十六进制,其他数字的表示均采用十进制。	All codes in the appendix are expressed in hexadecimal, and all other numbers are expressed in decimal.	no
单字节部分采用 GB/T 11383 一 1989 的编码结构,使 用 0x00~0x7F 码位。	The single-byte portion uses the GB/T 11383 1989 coding structure, using 0x00~0x7F code bits.	no
双字贡部分采用两个八位二进制位串表示一个字符,其首字节码位从 0x81 一 0xFE, 尾字节码位分别是 0x40 一 0x7E 和 0x80 一 0xFE。	The double glyph section uses two 8-bit binary bit strings to represent a character. The first byte is 0x81 one 0xFE, and the last byte is 0x40 one 0x7E and 0x80 one 0xFE, respectively.	no
四字节部分采用 GB/工 11383 一 1989 未采用的 0x30 一 0x39 作为对双字节编码扩充的后缀,编码范围为 0x81308130 一 0xFE39FE39。	The four-byte portion uses 0x30 one 0x39, which was not used in GB/work 11383 one 1989, as a suffix to double byte coding. The coding range is 0x81308130 one 0xFE39FE39.	no
四字节字符的第一个字厄编码范围为 0x81 一 0xFE;第二个字记编码范围为 0x30 一 0x39; 第三个字节编码范围为 0x81 一 0xFE;第 四个字市编码范围为 0x30 一 0x39。 即 : 0x81308130 一 0x81308139; 0x81308230 一 0x81308239 0x8130FEFE30 一 0x8130FE39 ; 0x81318130 一 0x81318139 ; Oo2douolag0c “0URo23061393 0xFE39FE30 一 0xFE39FE39 。	The first character code range of the four-byte character is 0x81 one 0xFE; the second character code range is 0x30 one 0x39; the third byte code range is 0x81 one 0xFE; and the fourth character code range is 0x30 one 0x39. Namely: 0x81308130 one 0x81308139; 0x81308230 one 0x81308239 0x8130fe30 0x8130fe39; 0x81318130 one 0x81318139; oo2duolag0c “0uro23061393 0xFE39FE30 one 0xFE39FE39.	no
总体结构与码位范围分配见图 1 和表 1。	The overall structure and bit range allocation are shown in Figure 1 and Table 1.	no
6 字符的排列顺序	The order in which the 6 characters are arranged	no
6.1 单字刷部分字符的排列顺序	6.1 The order of some characters in the single-word brush	no
单字记部分字符按照 GB/I 11383 一 1989 中相应字符的顺序排列 。	Some of the characters in the monolayer are arranged in the order of the corresponding characters in GB/I 11383 to 1989.	no
6.2 双字市部分字符的排列顺序	6.2 The order of some characters in the double character market	no
双字下部分字符排列顺序应符合附录 A。	The order of the characters below the double letter should match Appendix A.	no
6.3 四字刷部分字符的排列顺序	6.3 The order of some characters in the four-character brush	no
自 0x81308130 至 0x8439FE39 共 50400 个码位,对应双字节部分未包括的所有 GB/T 13000 基本多文种平面的字符,按照GB/T13000 基本多文种平面相应字符的顺序排列 。	From 0x81308130 to 0x8439FE39, there are a total of 50400 code bits corresponding to the double-byte portion of the GB/T 13000 basic multilingual plane, arranged in the order of the corresponding characters in the GB/T13000 basic multilingual plane.	no
自 0x90308130 至 0xE339FE39 共 1058400 个码位用于对应 GB/T 13000 的16个辅助平面,字符排列顺序完全按照 GB/I 13000 的 16个辅助平面的相应码位顺序依次排列 。	A total of 1058400 code bits from 0x90308130 to 0xE339FE39 are used on the 16 auxiliary planes corresponding to GB/T 13000. The character arrangement order is arranged exactly according to the order of the corresponding code bits of the 16 auxiliary planes of GB/I 13000.	no
四字节部分字符排列顺序应符合附录 C。	The four-byte portion of the characters should be in the same order as Appendix C.	no

9.1 通则	9.1 General Rules	yes
本文件规定三个实现级别。	This document specifies three levels of implementation.	yes
符合相应实现级别的系统软件产品,应提供相应实现级别范围内全部字符的输入输出功能。	System software products that meet the corresponding implementation level shall provide input and output functions for all characters within the corresponding implementation level range.	yes
9.2 实现级别 1	9.2 Implementing Level 1	yes
实现级别 1 文持本文件的单字节编码部分、双季节编码部分和四字下编玛部分的 CJK 统一汉字 ( 即 0x82358F33 一 0x82359636) 和 CJK 统一汉字扩A( 即 0x8139EE39 一 0x82358738) 。	Implement CJK unified Chinese characters (i.e. 0x82358F33 one 0x82359636) and CJK unified Chinese character expansion A (that is, 0x8139EE39 one 0x82358738) of the single-byte coding part, the two-season coding part, and the four-character under-letter word for level 1 text.	yes
任何本文件适用的产品均应满足实现级别 1 的要求。	Any product to which this document applies should meet the requirements for implementing Level 1.	yes
注: 根据软件应用需要 ,实现级别 1 还可选择文持表 3 列出的任何一种或多种非汉字文种。	NOTE: Depending on the requirements of the software application, Level 1 implementation can also select any one or more of the non-Chinese writing styles listed in Writing Table 3.	no
9.3 实现级别 2	9.3 Implementing Level 2	no
实现级别 2 包含实现级别 1。	Implementation level 2 includes implementation level 1.	no
此外 ,实现级别 2 还文持《通用 规范 汉字 表 }中的没有包合在实级别 1 之内的编码汉字。	Furthermore, implementation level 2 also maintains that there are no coded Chinese characters included within actual level 1 in the “General Standard Chinese Character List}”.	no
《 通用规范汉字表) 所收汉字在本文件中的代码位置和字形, 见附录下。	See the appendix for the code locations and glyphs of the Chinese characters included in the “General Standard Chinese Character List” in this document.	no
系统软件及支撑软件,应满足实现级别 2 的要求 。	The system software and supporting software shall meet the requirements for achieving Level 2.	no
注: 系统软件及文撑软件包括但不限于操作系统,数据库管理系统.中间件( 软件产品分类的信息见 GB/ 工 36475)。	Note: System software and documentation support software include, but are not limited to, operating systems, database management systems, middleware (see GB/ Engineering 36475 for software product classification information).	no
9.4 实现级别 3	9.4 Achieve Level 3	no
实现级别 3 包含实现级别 2。	Implementation level 3 includes implementation level 2.	no
此外,实现级别 3 还文持本文件规定的全部汉字及表 3 中的康黑部首。	Furthermore, to achieve level 3, the text also holds all of the Chinese characters specified in this document and the kang and black radicals in Table 3.	no
用于政务服务和公共服务的产品应满足实现级卉 3 的要求。	Products used in government services and public services shall meet the requirements for achieving Level 3.	no
注: 政务服务和 共服务行业包括但不限于铁路运输业.道路运输业 \ 水上运输业.航空运输业、多式联运和运输代理业、邮政业、货币金融服、保险业、土地、管理业、卫生、国家机构、社会保障等 (行业分类的信息见 GB/ 工 4754)。	Note: Government services and common service industries include, but are not limited to, rail transport, road transport\ water transport, air transport, multimodal transport and transport agencies, postal services, insurance, land, management, health, state institutions, social security, etc. (see GB/ Labor 4754 for industry classification information).	no

If you're only operating part of the four stages (preprocessing, compilation, assembly, connection), you can use the '-x' option (or Ah after the file name) to tell geo where to start, use the `~-c', or `-E' option to tell geo where to end. 编译后即停止, 不进行汇编件.	Once compiled, it stops; no assembly is carried out.	yes
在编译过程的不同阶段间使用管道而非临时文件进行工作, 因为那些系统的汇编器不能从管道读取数据，GNU 的汇编器没有这个问题，汇编器能够接受的 C "方言 ": 支持符合 ANSI 标准的 C 程序.	Pipelines rather than temporary files are used to work between the different stages of the compilation process, since those systems' assemblers can't read data from pipes. The GNU assembler doesn't have this problem. The assembler can accept the C “dialect”: supports C programs that conform to ANSI standards.	yes
这样就会关闭 GNU Cc 中某些不兼容 ANSI Cc 的特性关键字, 以及诸如 unix 和 vax 这些表明当迎和极少使用的 ANSI trigraph 特性,以及禁上尽管使 用了(译注 :宿主环境 (hosted environment) 下所有的标准库可用，main 函数返回 一个 int 值, 典型例子是除了内核以外几乎所有的程序.对应的独立环境 (f£reestanding environment) 不存在标准库, 程序入口也不一定是 main, 最明显的例子就是操作系统内核.详情参考 gcc 网站最近的资料)	This will turn off some feature keywords in GNU Cc that aren't compatible with ANSI Cc, as well as ANSI trigraph features such as unix and vax, which indicate that they are popular and rarely used, as well as disabling (note: all standard libraries are available in the hosted environment (hosted environment), and the function returns an int value for almost every program other than the kernel. The typical example is almost every program other than the kernel. The corresponding independent environment (f£) (Reestanding environment) There is no standard library, and the program entry is not necessarily main. The most obvious example is the operating system kernel. For details, see recent information on the GCC website)	yes
对于没有参数的函数声明, 例如 `int foo ();', 按 C 风格处理 --- 即不说明参数个数或类型. (仅针对 C++) .	Function declarations with no arguments, such as `int foo (); ', are treated in C style --- that is, the number or type of parameters is not specified. (For C++ only).	no
正常情况下, 这样的函数 foo 在 C++ 中意味着参数为空.	Under normal circumstances, a function like this foo in C++ means that the parameter is empty.	no
节清单从这里删到试图支持传统 C 编译器的某些方面.	The list of sections has been removed from here to some aspects that attempt to support the traditional C compiler.	no
详见NU c 手册,我们已经把细节删除, 这样当内容过时后, 人们也不会 HERI.	See the NU c manual for details; we've removed the details so that when the content is out of date, people won't be HERI.	no
除了一件事: 对于 c++ 程序 (不是C)，` -traditional' 选项带来一个附加效应,允许对 this 赋值.	Except for one thing: for C++ programs (not C), the '-traditional' option has an added effect, allowing values to be assigned to this.	no
他和`-Ethis-is-variable' 选项的果一样.	It has the same effect as the '-ethis-is-variable' option.	no
-traditional-cpp 试图支持传统 Cc 预处理器的某些方面.	-traditional-cpp attempts to support some aspects of the traditional CC preprocessor.	no
特别是上面提到有关预处理器的内容, 但是不包括 `-traditional' 选项的其他效应.	In particular, what is mentioned above about preprocessors is not included, but the other effects of the `-traditional' option are not included.	no
-fdollars-in-identifiers 允许在标识符 (identifier) 中使用 `$' 字符 (仅针对 C++) .	-fdollars-in-identifiers allows the use of the '$' character in identifiers (for C++ only).	no
你可以指定 `“-Efno-dollars-in-identifiers' 选项显明禁止使用 `$' 符.	You can specify the `"-efno-dollars-in-identifiers' option to explicitly disallow the use of the '$' character.	no
(GNU C++ 在某些目标系统缺省允许 `$' 符, 但不是所有系统.)	(GNU C++ allows the '$' character by default on some target systems, but not all systems.)	no
-fenum-int-equiv 允许 ant 类型到枚举类型 (enumeration) 的隐式转换 (MEF c++) .	-fenum-int-equiv allows implicit conversion of ant types to enumerated types (enumeration) (MEF c++).	no
正常情况下 GNU C++ 允许从 enum 到 int 的转换,反之则不行.	Under normal circumstances, GNU C++ allows conversion from enum to int; the reverse is not possible.	no
-fexternal-—templates 为模板声明 (template declaration) 产生较小的代码 (仅限于 c++)，方法是对于每个模板函数 (template function),只在 定义他们的地方生成一个副本.	-fexternal-—templates generates smaller code (c++ only) for template declarations (template declarations) by generating a copy of each template function (template function) only where they are defined.	no
想要成功使用这个选项, 你必须在所有使用模板的文件中,标记`#pragma implementatio'(定义)或 `#Pragma interface'(声明).	To successfully use this option, you must mark either `#pragma implementation tatio' (definition) or `#Pragma interface' (statement) in all files using the template.	no
程序用 `-fexternal-templates ' 编译时, 模板实例 (template instantiation) 全部是外部类型.你必须让需要的实例在实现文件中出现.	When a program is compiled with `-fexternal-templates', all template instantiations (template instantiations) are external types. You must make the required instances appear in the implementation file.	no
可以通过 typedef 实现这一点, 他引用所需的每个实例.	This can be achieved through typedef, which refers to every instance required.	no
相对应的, 如果编译时使用缺省选项 ` -fno-exteznal-templates', 所有模板实例明确的设为内置.	Correspondence, if the default option `-fno-exteznal-templates' is used at compile time, all template instances are explicitly set as built-in.	no
所有的成员函数(除了构造子函数和 mnew 或 delete 成员操作符) 视为所在类的虚函数.	All member functions (with the exception of constructor subfunctions and the mnew or delete member operators) are considered virtual functions of the class in which they belong.	no
这不表明每次调用成员函数都将通过内部虚函数表.	This doesn't indicate that every call to a member function will go through the internal virtual function table.	no
有些情况下, 编译器能够判断出可以直接调用某个虚函数; 这时就直接调用.	In some cases, the compiler can determine that a virtual function can be called directly; at this point, it is called directly.	no
-fcond-mismatch 允许条件表达式的第二和第三个参数的类型不匹配.	-fcond-mismatch allows the types of the second and third parameters of the conditional expression to not match.	no
这种表达式的值是 Void.-fthis-—is-variable 允许对 this 赋值 (仅对 c++).	The value of this type of expression is Void. -fthis-—is-variable allows assigning values to this (for c++ only).	no
合并用户自定义的自由存储管理机制到 c++ 后,使可赋值的`this' 显得不合时宜.	Incorporating a user-defined free storage management mechanism into C++ makes the “this” that can be assigned a value seem out of place.	no
因此, 默认情况下, 类成员函数内部对 this 赋值是无效操作.	Therefore, by default, assigning a value to this from within a class member function is an invalid operation.	no
然而为了向后兼容, 你可以通过 `-fthis-is-variable' 选项使这种操作有效.	However, for backwards compatibility, you can make this operation effective with the `-fthis-is-variable' option.	no
-funsigned-char 把 char 定义为无符号类型,如同 unsigned char.	-funsigned-char defines a char as an unsigned type, just like an unsigned char.	no
各种机器都有自己缺省的 char 类型. 既可能是 unsigned char 也可能是 signed char.	Every machine has its own default char type. It could be either an unsigned char or a signed char.	no
理想情况下, 当依赖于数据的符号性时, 一个可移植程序总是应该使用 signed char 或 unsigned chaz.	Ideally, when relying on the symbolic nature of the data, a portable program should always use signed char or unsigned chaz.	no
但是许多程序已经写成只用简单的 char, 并且期街这是有符号数(或者无符号数, 具体情况取决于编写程序的目标机器).	But many programs have been written using only a simple char, and the expectation street is a signed number (or an unsigned number, depending on the target machine that wrote the program).	no
这个选项, 和它的反义选项, 使那样的程序工作在对应的默认值上.	This option, and its antonym, makes such programs work on the corresponding default values.	no
char 的类型始终应该明确定义为 signed char 或 unsigned char, 即使它表现的和其中之一完全一样.	The type of char should always be clearly defined as signed char or unsigned char, even if it represents exactly one of them.	no
如果没有明确声明 ` signed' 或 "unsigned'修饰符, 这些选项用来定义有符号位域 (bitfield) 或无符号位域.	If no 'signed' or “unsigned” modifiers are explicitly stated, these options are used to define a signed bitfield (bitfield) or an unsigned bitfield.	no
缺省情况下,位域是有符号的, 因为他们继承的基本整数类型,如 int,是有符号数，然而, 如果指定了 `-traditional' 选项,位域永远是无符号数.	By default, bitfields are signed, since the basic integer types they inherit, such as int, are signed numbers; however, if the `-traditional' option is specified, the bitfields are always unsigned numbers.	no
-fwritable-strings把字符串常量存储到可写数据段, 而且不做特别对待.	-fwritable-strings stores string constants in a writable data section without any special treatment.	no
这是为了兼容一些老程序,他们算改字符串常量是一个非常糟糕的想法、`-traditional' 选项也有相同效果.	This is to be compatible with some old programs; their calculation of string constants is a very bad idea, and the '-traditional' option has the same effect.	no
执行摘要	Executive summary	yes
新冠肺炎对毒品市场的影响	The impact of COVID-19 on the drug market	yes
其影响可能类似于2008年的经济危机	The impact could be similar to the 2008 economic crisis	yes
全球性的新冠肺炎疫情已使全世界陷入前所未有的危机。	The global COVID-19 pandemic has plunged the world into an unprecedented crisis.	yes
在许多国家，这一疾病己使医疗服务机构穷于应付，几近崩溃，各国政府实施的限制措施已在全球经济中造成了严重紊乱。	In many countries, the disease has left health-care institutions too poor to handle and has nearly collapsed, and restrictions imposed by governments have caused serious disruptions in the global economy.	yes
对于毒品市场，这场疫情的影响尚不清楚，也很难预测，但有可能影响深远。	As for the drug market, the impact of the pandemic is unclear and difficult to predict, but it is likely to have far-reaching effects.	yes
一些生产者可能会被迫寻找新的方法来制造毒品，因为限制流动的同时也限制了前体和基本化学品的获取。	Some producers may be forced to find new ways to manufacture drugs, as both movement restrictions limit access to precursors and essential chemicals.	yes
贩运者由于旅行限制而无法越境，可能不得不寻找新的路线和方法。	Traffickers are unable to cross the border due to travel restrictions and may have to find new routes and methods.	yes
毒品使用和提供的模式可能会改变，政府的应对能力也可能会受到阻碍。	Patterns of drug use and delivery may change, and the government's ability to respond may be hampered.	yes
新冠肺炎带来的转变是前所未有的，但还是可以从以往的危机中吸取一些经验教训。	The transformation brought about by COVID-19 is unprecedented, but we can still learn some lessons from past crises.	yes
2008年经济危机后，一些吸毒者开始寻找更便宜的合成物质，使用模式转向注射毒品。	After the 2008 economic crisis, some drug users began searching for cheaper synthetic substances and switched their usage pattern to injecting drugs.	no
与此同时，各国政府削减了与毒品相关的预算。	At the same time, governments have cut drug-related budgets.	no
如果各国政府以同样的方式应对当前的经济衰退，预防吸毒和相关风险行为等干预措施和戒毒治疗服务可能会受到沉重打击。	If governments respond in the same way to the current economic downturn, interventions to prevent drug use and related risk behaviors and drug treatment services could be hit hard.	no
此外，拦截行动和国际合作的优先性可能会降低，使贩运者更容易行动。	Furthermore, interdiction operations and international cooperation may be given less priority, making it easier for traffickers to act.	no
一些国家有大量毒品通过商业航班走私，预计这些国家的贩毒活动受到的直接影响最大。	A number of countries have large amounts of drugs smuggled through commercial flights, and drug trafficking activities in these countries are expected to be the most directly affected.	no
有信使将甲基苯丙胺等合成毒品放在随身背包或藏在私人行李中携带，有时数量很大。由于几乎各地都对航空客运实施了限制，利用商业航空旅行供应毒品的活动可能会完全中断。	Couriers carry synthetic drugs such as methamphetamine in carry-on backpacks or in personal luggage, sometimes in large quantities. As restrictions on air passenger traffic are imposed almost everywhere, activities using commercial air travel to supply drugs may be completely interrupted.	no
尽管国际邮政供应链也受到了干扰，但利用暗网和货物邮寄进行贩运的活动可能会增加。	Although the international postal supply chain has also been disrupted, the use of the dark web and the mailing of goods for trafficking is likely to increase.	no
从长远来看，经济衰退和相关的封闭措施可能会打乱毒品市场。	In the long run, the economic downturn and associated lockdown measures could disrupt the drug market.	no
由于不断上升的失业率和缺乏机会，贫困和弱势人群将更有可能以有害的方式吸毒，患上吸毒病症，并转向与毒品有关的非法活动一无论是生产还是运输。	Due to rising unemployment and lack of opportunities, poor and vulnerable people will be more likely to use drugs in harmful ways, develop drug addiction disorders, and switch to illegal drug-related activities, whether production or transportation.	no
贩毒组织可能会利用这种情况，向脆弱人群提供服务，并招募新成员来壮大队伍。	Drug cartels may take advantage of this situation to provide services to vulnerable people and recruit new members to grow their ranks.	no
随着政府应对能力的降低，这些转变可能会快速扎根，成为许多社区的新现实。	As the government's ability to respond declines, these changes are likely to quickly take root and become a new reality for many communities.	no
扩张与复杂性	Expansion and Complexity	no
市场增长	Market growth	no
人口增长模式部分解释了市场扩张的原因	The population growth pattern partly explains the reasons for market expansion	no
世界各地的吸毒现象一直在增多，无论是从总体数字还是从吸毒者在世界人口中所占比例来看都是如此。	Drug use has been increasing all over the world, both in terms of overall numbers and in terms of the proportion of drug users in the world population.	no
2009年估计吸毒者有2.1亿人，占全球15-64岁人口的4.8%,而2018年估计吸毒者有2.69亿人，占这类人口的5.3%。	In 2009, there were an estimated 210 million drug users, accounting for 4.8% of the global population aged 15-64, while the estimated number of drug users in 2018 was 269 million, accounting for 5.3% of this population.	no
在过去二十年期间，发展中国家吸毒情况的增长速度远远快于发达国家。	Over the past two decades, drug use in developing countries has grown far faster than developed countries.	no
这在一定程度上反映了这一期间总体人口增长的差异、发达国家为7%,发展中国家为28%但也反映了发展中国家年 轻人口增长较快。	This partly reflects the difference in overall population growth during this period, with developed countries at 7% and developing countries at 28%, but it also reflects the faster growth of the young population in developing countries.	no
青少年和年轻成年人在吸毒者中所占比例最大。	Adolescents and young adults make up the largest proportion of drug users.	no
在2000-2018年期间，发展中国家这一年龄段的人口增长了16%,而发达国家这一年龄段的人口减少了10%。	Between 2000 and 2018, the population of this age group in developing countries increased by 16%, while the population of this age group in developed countries declined by 10%.	no
1城市化是当前和未来毒品市场的一个驱动因素	1 Urbanization is a driver of current and future drug markets	no
无论是发达国家还是发展中国家，城市地区的吸毒情况都多于农村地区。	In both developed and developing countries, there is more drug use in urban areas than in rural areas.	no
吸毒情况总体增多的部分原因是人口从农村向城镇的大规模流动一目前全世界人口有一半以上生活在城市地区，而1960年这一比例为34%。	The overall increase in drug use is partly due to the large-scale movement of people from rural to urban1 Currently, more than half of the world's population lives in urban areas, compared to 34% in 1960.	no
城市化可能是毒品市场未来动态的一个关键因素，特别是在城市化趋势更为突出的发展中国家。	Urbanization may be a key factor in the future dynamics of drug markets, particularly in developing countries where urbanization trends are more pronounced.	no
财富的增加与吸毒情况增多相联，但承受疾病负担最大的是最贫穷的人在世界范围内，发达国家的吸毒情况比发展中国家更为普遍。	Increased wealth is linked to increased drug use, yet the poorest people bear the greatest burden of disease worldwide, and drug use is more common in developed countries than in developing countries.	no
可卡因之类的毒品更是与世界上较富裕的地区联系较为牢固。	Drugs such as cocaine are even more strongly linked to the wealthiest regions of the world.	no
同样，在各国内部，社会富裕阶层的吸毒流行率较高。	Similarly, within countries, the prevalence of drug use is higher among the affluent sectors of society.	no
但转为吸毒病症的比率较高的却是社会经济地位较低的人。	However, those with lower socioeconomic status have a higher rate of conversion to drug addiction.	no
来自少数几个国家的数据表明，有害的吸毒模式与病症同低收入之间存在联系。	Data from a few countries suggest a link between harmful drug use patterns and illness and low income.	no
这些模式在较富裕的社会阶层似乎不太常见。	These patterns seem to be less common in the more affluent social classes.	no
全球新冠肺炎危机造成的经济制约很可能会加剧包括吸毒者在内的最弱势群体的风险。	The economic constraints caused by the global COVID-19 crisis are likely to heighten the risks of the most vulnerable groups, including drug users.	no
例如，劳动力市场的变化，如失业率上升，过去一直与吸毒情况的增加有关，而这场疫情己经迫使全球数千万人失业。	For example, changes in the labor market, such as rising unemployment, have been linked to increased drug use in the past, and the pandemic has already forced tens of millions of people around the world to lose their jobs.	no
新冠肺炎或将导致毒品市场进一步扩张新冠肺炎的大流行可能会导致更多农民增加或从事非法作物种植，或是因为国家主管机关的控制能力降低，或是因为在经济危机之下可能有更多人不得不铤而走险，从事非法活动。	COVID-19 may cause the drug market to expand further. The COVID-19 pandemic may cause more farmers to increase or engage in illegal crop cultivation, or because of reduced control capacity of national authorities, or because more people may have to take risks and engage in illegal activities under the economic crisis.	no
新冠肺炎的相关限制措施导致空中和陆路交通减少，海上贩运可能已经因此而增加，海上的拦截风险低，而且比空中或陆路走私的数量更多。	The restrictions associated with COVID-19 have led to a reduction in air and land traffic, and maritime trafficking may have increased as a result. The risk of interception at sea is low, and there is more volume than air or land smuggling.	no
最近已有报告称可卡因货物直接从南美经由海路运往欧洲。	There have been recent reports of cocaine shipments directly from South America to Europe by sea.	no
复杂性增强	Increased complexity	yes
非国际管制物质的出现情况稳定，但有潜在危害的新型类阿片正在增多毒品市场正日趋复杂。	The emergence of substances not under international control is stable, but potentially harmful novel opioid types are increasing, and the drug market is becoming increasingly complex.	yes
除大麻、可卡因和海洛因等植物类物质之外，已经增添了数百种合成毒品，其中许多并不在国际管制之下。药品的非医疗使用也快速增多。	In addition to plant-based substances such as cannabis, cocaine, and heroin, hundreds of synthetic drugs have been added, many of which are not under international control. Non-medical use of pharmaceuticals is also rapidly increasing.	yes
会员国的国内市场每年约有500种新型活性物质。	Member States' domestic markets have around 500 novel active substances each year.	yes
目前其中大多是兴奋剂，其次是合成的大麻素受体激动剂和少量的类阿片。	Currently, most of them are stimulants, followed by synthetic cannabinoid agonists and small amounts of opioids.	yes
虽然新型精神活性物质的总体数量已经稳定下来，但比例发生了变化。	Although the overall amount of novel psychoactive substances has stabilized, the proportions have changed.	yes
在2014年确定的新型精神活性物质种类总数中，类阿片新型精神活性物质仅占2%,但到2018年，这一数字己上升至9%。	Novel opioid psychoactive substances accounted for only 2% of the total number of novel psychoactive substances identified in 2014, but by 2018, this figure had risen to 9%.	yes
类阿片新型精神活性物质中有许多是芬太尼的类似物，其药效和危害已得到证明，在北美导致了过量死亡事件，其他区域也有，但程度较轻。	Many of the novel opioid psychoactive substances are fentanyl analogues. Their efficacy and harm have been proven to have caused overdose deaths in North America, as well as in other regions, but to a lesser extent.	yes
在北美，芬太尼有的用作海洛因和其他毒品（包括可卡因和甲基苯丙胺）的掺杂剂，有的用来制造假冒的药用类阿片。	In North America, some fentanyl is used as a doping agent for heroin and other drugs, including cocaine and methamphetamine, while others are used to make counterfeit pharmaceutical opioids.	yes
一些证据表明，欧洲也有注射新型精神活性物质兴奋剂的现象：一项对欧洲六个城市废弃注射器残留物的研宄发现，许多注射器都沾有产生兴奋作用的新型精神活性物质》	Some evidence suggests that Europe also has the phenomenon of doping with novel psychoactive substances: a study on the residues of abandoned syringes in six European cities found that many syringes contained novel psychoactive substances with stimulatory effects.”	yes
2新型精神活性物质的使用可能会逐渐牢固存在于弱势群体中	2 The use of novel psychoactive substances may gradually become entrenched in vulnerable groups	no
单一种类的新型精神活性物质几乎从未形成大的市场。	A single class of novel psychoactive substances has almost never formed a large market.	no
但来自欧洲的证据表明，合成大麻素在无家可归者和监狱囚犯等社会边缘群体中是一个严重的问题。	But evidence from Europe suggests that synthetic cannabinoids are a serious problem among marginalized groups such as homeless people and prison inmates.	no
有22个国家报告了监狱中使用新型精神活性物质的情况，其中大多数国家将合成大麻素确定为主要挑战。	Twenty-two countries reported on the use of novel psychoactive substances in prisons, most of which identified synthetic cannabinoids as a major challenge.	no
对前体化学品的管制迫使制毒者进行创新最常作为前体用来合成苯丙胺、甲基苯丙胺和“摇头丸”等毒品的许多化学品已被置于国际管制之下。	Control of precursor chemicals forces drug makers to innovate Many of the chemicals most commonly used as precursors to synthesize drugs such as amphetamine, methamphetamine, and “ecstasy” have been placed under international control.	no
贩毒者和制毒者一直在寻找替代品一不仅有管制较松的物质，还有专门为规避管制而设计的化学品，即所谓的“特制前体”。	Drug traffickers and drug producers are always looking for alternatives, not only less controlled substances, but also chemicals specifically designed to evade control, so-called “special precursors.”	no
旨在阻止新冠肺炎传播的限制性措施很可能使依赖前体化学品的制毒者受到进一步挤压。	Restrictive measures aimed at stopping the spread of COVID-19 are likely to further squeeze drug makers that rely on precursor chemicals.	no
来自墨西哥的证据表明，这已经成为 现实：据报告，2020年3月，从东亚进口的甲基苯丙胺前体短缺促使墨西哥和美国的甲基苯丙胺价格上涨。	Evidence from Mexico suggests this is already a reality: in March 2020, a shortage of methamphetamine precursors imported from East Asia reportedly prompted a rise in methamphetamine prices in Mexico and the US.	no
市场瞬息万变	The market is changing rapidly	no
合成药物在中亚和俄罗斯联邦取代阿片剂	Synthetic drugs replace opiates in Central Asia and the Russian Federation	no
中亚和俄罗斯联邦的阿片剂市场在2008年至2018年期间似乎发生了变化。	The opiates market in Central Asia and the Russian Federation appears to have changed between 2008 and 2018.	no
俄罗斯联邦当局截获的阿片剂数量下降了约80%，同时因使用类阿片而接受治疗的人数大幅减少。	The number of opiates intercepted by Russian authorities has dropped by about 80 per cent, while the number of people receiving treatment for opioid use has been drastically reduced.	no
但兴奋剂市场却似乎日渐兴旺。	But the doping market seems to be booming.	no
有证据表明，甲基苯丙胺和各种卡西酮，包括甲氧麻黄酮和 a - 吡咯烷基苯戊酮，现在俄罗斯毒品市场上随处可见。	There is evidence that methamphetamine and various cathinones, including methephedrone and a-pyrrolidinylphenylpentanone, are now ubiquitous in the Russian drug market.	no
俄罗斯当局报告称，最近查获的制造各种非法药物的秘密加工点数量急剧上升，在两年内翻了一番多，2018年增至152个加工点。	Russian authorities report that the number of recently seized clandestine processing sites that manufacture various illegal drugs has risen sharply, more than doubled in two years, to 152 processing sites in 2018.	no
阿富汗和伊拉克甲基苯丙胺市场增长	Growth in methamphetamine markets in Afghanistan and Iraq	no
早在2012年，对医院、监狱和其他机构人员的调查就已经揭示了甲基苯丙胺在伊拉克的重要性。	As early as 2012, surveys of personnel in hospitals, prisons and other institutions had revealed the importance of methamphetamine in Iraq.	no
结晶甲基苯丙胺已经成为“芬乃他林”和曲马多之外又一种令人担忧的主要药物。	Crystalline methamphetamine has become another worrisome major drug other than “fennethalin” and tramadol.	no
2015年的一项研宄进一步证实了这些发现，吸毒者表示大麻比“芬乃他林”或甲基苯丙胺更难获得。	A 2015 study further confirmed these findings, with drug users saying marijuana is harder to obtain than “fennethalin” or methamphetamine.	no
最近，伊拉克当局发现了多个甲基苯丙胺加工点，麻管局已对伪麻黄碱制剂的大批进口表示关切一甲基苯丙胺加工点将这些制剂用作前体。	Recently, the Iraqi authorities discovered multiple methamphetamine processing sites, and the Board has expressed concern over the massive import of pseudoephedrine preparations using these agents as precursors at a methamphetamine processing site.	no
在阿富汗，甲基苯丙胺制造似乎始于2014年。	In Afghanistan, methamphetamine production appears to have started in 2014.	no
自那时起，甲基苯丙胺的缉获量一直在稳步上升。	Since then, there has been a steady rise in methamphetamine seizures.	no
但2019年上半年的缉获量一^657公斤——与上一年相比大幅骤增。	But the amount seized in the first half of 2019 was 1,^657 kg — a sharp increase from the previous year.	no
在其他国家大量缉获了据认为源自阿富汗的甲基苯丙胺，这也表明该国的产量正在迅速上升。	Large amounts of methamphetamine believed to have originated in Afghanistan have been seized in other countries, which also indicates that the country's production is rising rapidly.	no
政策变化和变化趋势	Policy changes and changing trends	yes
非医疗使用大麻合法化的法域大多有大麻使用增多的趋势	Most of the jurisdictions that have legalized the non-medical use of marijuana have a trend of increasing marijuana use	yes
加拿大、乌拉圭和美国的11个法域允许制造大麻产品供非医疗使用。	Eleven jurisdictions in Canada, Uruguay, and the United States allow the manufacture of cannabis products for non-medical use.	yes
在其中多数法域，大麻使用自合法化以来有所增多，尽管在其他未将非医疗使用大麻合法化的法域也观察到了同样的趋势。	Cannabis use has increased in most of these jurisdictions since legalization, although similar trends have been observed in other jurisdictions that have not legalized non-medical use of marijuana.	yes
在美国最早通过立法的两个州科罗拉多州和华盛顿州，成年人非医疗使用大麻的情况增加，特别是过去一个月以及每天或几乎每天使用的情况增多，自2012年起便已超过了全国平均水平。	In Colorado and Washington, the first two states to pass legislation in the US, there has been an increase in non-medical use of marijuana among adults, particularly over the past month and the increase in daily or almost daily use, which has surpassed the national average since 2012.	yes
所有指标都显示，自2011年以来，乌拉圭的大麻使用情况有所增加，上月使用情况几乎翻了一番。	All indicators show that cannabis use in Uruguay has increased since 2011, almost doubling last month.	yes
这表明增加的主要原因是经常和频繁使用大麻。	This indicates that the increase is mainly due to the frequent and frequent use of marijuana.	yes
加拿大的短期数据也表明，2018年至2019年合法市场扩大的同时，使用量也在增加。	Canada's short-term data also shows that while the legal market expanded from 2018 to 2019, usage also increased.	yes
然而，2019年仍有40%的大麻使用者靠非法来源获得某些产品。	However, 40% of cannabis users still obtained certain products from illegal sources in 2019.	yes
全球大麻药草缉获量暴跌的背后原因是大麻合法化？	Is the reason behind the sharp drop in global cannabis herb seizures the legalization of marijuana?	yes
2018年，全球大麻药草缉获量降至20年来的最低水平，这是因为北美的缉获量下降，在过去10年中下降了 84%。	In 2018, global cannabis herb seizures fell to their lowest level in 20 years due to declining seizures in North America, which fell 84% over the past 10 years.	no
相比之下，同期世界其他地区的缉获量几乎翻了一番。缉获的模式表明，旨在放开大麻市场的政策在下降中发挥了关键作用。	By contrast, the volume of seizures in other parts of the world almost doubled during the same period. Seizure patterns suggest that policies aimed at liberalizing the cannabis market played a key role in the decline.	no
对新型精神活性物质的监管似乎有遏制作用在国内对新型精神活性物质的监管效果仍然很难评估。	The regulation of novel psychoactive substances appears to have a curbing effect. It is still difficult to evaluate the effects of domestic regulation of novel psychoactive substances.	no
一些对新型精神活性物质采用不同监管制度的国家显示出不同的新型精神活性物质使用流行率。	Some countries with different regulatory systems for novel psychoactive substances have shown different prevalence rates of novel psychoactive substance use.	no
在另一些国家，通过国内立法后，新型精神活性物质使用情况有所减少。	In other countries, there has been a decrease in the use of novel psychoactive substances after the adoption of domestic legislation.	no
弱势群体面临合法和非法毒品市场的伤害用于疼痛管理和姑息治疗的药用类阿片主要在高收入国家提供止痛药在各区域分布不均。	Vulnerable groups face damage from the legal and illegal drug markets. Medicinal opioids used for pain management and palliative treatment mainly provide pain relievers in high-income countries and are unevenly distributed across regions.	no
2018年，所有可供医疗消费的药用类阿片中，90%以上在高收入国家。	In 2018, over 90% of all pharmaceutical opioids available for medical consumption were in high-income countries.	no
大约50%在北美，40%在欧洲，还有2%在大洋洲。	About 50% are in North America, 40% are in Europe, and 2% are in Oceania.	no
这些国家的人口约占全球人口的12%。	These countries account for about 12% of the global population.	no
据估计，低收入和中等收入国家的人口占全球人口的88%,但消费的药用类阿片却不到10%。	It is estimated that low- and middle-income countries make up 88% of the global population, yet consume less than 10% of pharmaceutical opioids.	no
获取药用类阿片的障碍与许多因素有关，包括立法、文化、卫生系统和处方做法。	Barriers to access to medicinal opioids are linked to many factors, including legislation, culture, health systems, and prescription practices.	no
较贫穷的人患吸毒病症的风险更大2018年约有3,560万人患有吸毒病症。	Poorer people are at greater risk of developing drug addiction disorders. In 2018, about 35.6 million people had drug addiction conditions.	no
贫困、有限的教育和社会边缘化可能会增加吸毒病症风险，并加剧其后果。高收入国家的研宄证实了这一点，在这些研究中，个人不利的社会经济轨迹一不仅仅是他们在某一时间点的状况一也与吸毒病症风险有关。	Poverty, limited education, and social marginalization may increase the risk of drug use diseases and exacerbate their consequences. Studies from high-income countries confirm this. In these studies, an individual's unfavorable socio-economic trajectory is not only related to their condition at a certain point in time, but also to the risk of drug addiction symptoms.	no
吸毒病症还会加深社会经济劣势，进一步增加失业、贫困和无家可归的风险，从而助长劣势的恶性循环。这些结果也可能与刑事司法系统内的侮辱性态度和后果有关。	Drug addiction also deepens socio-economic disadvantages and further increases the risk of unemployment, poverty, and homelessness, thereby fueling a vicious cycle of disadvantage. These results may also be related to abusive attitudes and consequences within the criminal justice system.	no
妇女、少数民族和移民、性取向多样化群体、因武装冲突或灾难而流离失所的人以及农村环境中的人也可能受到吸毒病症的过重影响，或者在获得治疗服务方面遇到问题。	Women, ethnic minorities and immigrants, sexually diverse groups, people displaced by armed conflict or disaster, and people in rural settings may also be disproportionately affected by drug use or have problems accessing treatment services.	no
根据估计因残疾和过早死亡而损失的健康寿命年数的残疾调整寿命年（DALY)指标，在过去10年中，有害的吸毒对范围更广的社会影响加重。	According to the Disability-Adjusted Life Span (DALY) index, which estimates the number of years of healthy life expectancy lost due to disability and premature death, the impact of harmful drug use on a wider range of societies has worsened over the past 10 years.	no
2007年至2018年间，归因于吸毒的全球残疾调整寿命年数增加了 17%。	Between 2007 and 2018, there was a 17 per cent increase in global disability-adjusted life expectancy due to drug use.	no
注射吸毒者中常见的未经治疗的丙型肝炎导致的肝癌的相关残疾调整寿命年数增幅特别高——达到40%。	Liver cancer associated with untreated hepatitis C, which is common among injecting drug users, increased the number of years of life expectancy was particularly high — up to 40%.	no
毒品和暴力之间的关系错综复杂很难确定精神活性物质的使用和暴力之间的所有因果关系。	The complex relationship between drugs and violence makes it difficult to determine all the causal relationships between psychoactive substance use and violence.	no
全球范围的有限数据表明，迷醉可能是杀人的一个重要因素。	Limited data from around the world suggest that intoxication may be a significant factor in homicides.	no
但在暴力事件中，酒精的作用似乎比毒品更大。	But alcohol appears to play a greater role than drugs in violent incidents.	no
虽然吸毒可能会导致犯罪，但在某些情况下，这种联系可以部分归因于多种中介因素，如社会经济劣势以及由个人风险、家庭环境和同龄人影响造成的其他类型的逆境。	Although drug use may lead to crime, in some cases this link may be due in part to a variety of mediating factors, such as socio-economic disadvantages and other types of adversity caused by personal risk, family environment, and peer influence.	no
贩毒和暴力之间的联系是多方面的。	The link between drug trafficking and violence is multifaceted.	no
如果已有稳定的犯罪结构，包括国际贩毒在内的大规模有组织犯罪活动有可能在无暴力的情况下实施。	If there is a stable criminal structure, large-scale organized crime, including international drug trafficking, is likely to be carried out without violence.	no
短期内，暴力的存在和程度与其说取决于贩运的数量，不如说取决于造成有组织犯罪集团之间力量平衡不稳定的某些变化，例如非法市场规模的变化，知名罪犯的死亡或监禁，以及使一个集团弱于另一个集团的执法措施。	In the short term, the existence and extent of violence depends not so much on the amount of trafficking as on certain changes that destabilize the balance of power among organized criminal groups, such as changes in the size of illegal markets, the death or imprisonment of well-known criminals, and enforcement measures that make one group weaker than another.	no
最新趋势	The latest trends	yes
吸毒大麻是最常用的物质，类阿片危害最大	Drug use of marijuana is the most commonly used substance, and opioids are the most harmful	yes
据估计，2018年使用大麻的有 1.92 亿人，使之成为全球使用最多的毒品。	It is estimated that 192 million people used marijuana in 2018, making it the most used drug in the world.	yes
相比之下，2018年使用类阿片的有5,800万人。	By contrast, 58 million people used opioids in 2018.	yes
但阿片类药物的相关危害却因使用者较少而受到忽视。	However, the harms associated with opioids have been ignored due to fewer users.	yes
在2017年与吸毒病症有关的估计167,000例死亡中，有66%是这类物质造成的，在据信为吸毒导致的残疾或过早死亡而损失的2,100万年寿命中，有50%是这类物质造成的。	Of the estimated 167,000 deaths associated with drug use conditions in 2017, 66% were caused by these substances, and 50% of the 21 million years of life believed to have been lost due to disability or premature death due to drug use were caused by these substances.	yes
合成类阿片的非医疗使用加剧了公共卫生危机	Non-medical use of synthetic opioids has exacerbated the public health crisis	yes
在西非、中部非洲和北非，加剧类阿片危机的是曲马多；在北美则是芬太尼。这两个区域在经济、人口统计数据或一般吸毒模式方面几乎没有共同点，但都在奋力抗击由容易获得且生产成本低的物质助长的类阿片危机。	In West Africa, Central Africa, and North Africa, it is tramadol that is exacerbating the opioid crisis; in North America it is fentanyl. The two regions have little in common in terms of economies, demographics, or general drug use patterns, yet they are struggling to fight the opioid crisis fueled by substances that are easily available and low in production costs.	yes
在北美，芬太尼等合成类阿片的使用导致了20年来类阿片过量致死人数增加。	In North America, the use of synthetic opioids such as fentanyl has led to an increase in the number of deaths due to opioid overdose over the past 20 years.	yes
2018年，在美国登记的67,367例过量死亡中，有三分之二涉及芬太尼。	In 2018, two-thirds of the 67,367 overdose deaths registered in the US involved fentanyl.	yes
加拿大也报告了类似的结果，只是数字较低。	Canada also reported similar results, but the numbers were lower.	no
芬太尼导致过量死亡的部分原因是非法药物市场上的芬太尼药效不可预测。	Part of the cause of fentanyl overdose deaths is the unpredictable efficacy of fentanyl on the illegal drug market.	no
在西非、中部非洲和北非，非医疗用途曲马多的市场已有大幅增长。	In West Africa, Central Africa, and North Africa, the market for non-medical use of tramadol has grown significantly.	no
在该区域，接受治疗的曲马多使用病症患者越来越多。	In this region, more and more patients with tramadol use conditions are being treated.	no
2017年，全球截获的曲马多数量显著增加，达到125吨以上的峰值。	In 2017, the majority of trout horses intercepted worldwide increased significantly, reaching a peak value of over 125 tons.	no
但2018年，在印度通过一项监管曲马多的新法律之后，全球缉获量降至32吨。	But in 2018, after India passed a new law regulating tramadol, global seizures fell to 32 tons.	no
促成这两地危机的是制造简单和生产成本低，此外还有对曲马多和许多芬太尼类似物或其前体缺乏国际监管。	What contributed to the crisis in these two places was the simplicity of manufacture and low production costs, in addition to the lack of international regulation of tramadol and many fentanyl analogues or their precursors.	no
使这两地危机恶化的是这些物质在药品市场和非法市场上都有供应，因而更加难以发现和防止其滥用。	What worsens the crisis in both places is that these substances are available in both drug markets and illegal markets, making it more difficult to detect and prevent their misuse.	no

根据所掌握的多数指标，20年来这两个区域甲基苯丙胺的使用一直在扩大。	According to most of the available indicators, the use of methamphetamine in these two regions has continued to expand over the past 20 years.	no
在一些市场上，可卡因和甲基苯丙胺可以共存，有时是相互替代，这样一种药物的使用量上升时另一种药物的使用量就下降，有时是同时增加和减少以满足同一市场的需求。	In some markets, cocaine and methamphetamine can coexist, sometimes replacing each other. As the usage of one drug increases, the use of another drug decreases, sometimes simultaneously increasing and decreasing to meet the needs of the same market.	no
新冠肺炎使注射吸毒者的风险增高	COVID-19 increases the risk of injecting drug users	no
据估计，2018年注射吸毒的约有1,130万人，全球艾滋病毒感染约有10%是注射吸毒造成的。	According to estimates, there were about 11.3 million injecting drug users in 2018, and about 10% of global HIV infections were caused by injecting drug use.	no
注射吸毒者感染艾滋病毒的超过100万人，患丙型肝炎的有550万人。	More than 1 million people are infected with HIV among injecting drug users, and 5.5 million people are infected with hepatitis C.	no

5 新冠肺炎限制措施造成的类阿片短缺可能导致使用者代之以酒精或苯二氮类药物等更容易获得的物质，或者将类阿片与合成药物混合。	5 Opioid shortages due to COVID-19 restrictions may cause users to replace more readily available substances such as alcohol or benzodiazepines, or mix opioids with synthetic drugs.	no

欧盟峰会为难民政策争吵不休，欧盟官员：接收过程每一步都存在瓶颈	EU summit bickers over refugee policy. EU official: There are bottlenecks at every step of the acceptance process	yes
【环球时报驻比利时特派记者 牛瑞飞】据法新社2月10日报道，在当天最新的一次欧盟峰会上，欧盟委员会主席冯德莱恩表示，欧盟领导人同意就非法移民问题出台更严格的政策，以此更易于驱逐非法移民。	[Niu Ruifei, Special Correspondent of the Global Times in Belgium] According to an AFP report on February 10, at the latest EU summit on the same day, European Commission President von der Leyen said that EU leaders agreed to introduce stricter policies on illegal immigration, making it easier to expel illegal immigrants.	yes

根据峰会文件，欧盟领导人呼吁委员会“立即调动大量欧盟资金”，以基础设施和监视等手段加强外部边界。	According to the summit documents, EU leaders called on the Commission to “immediately mobilize large amounts of EU funds” to strengthen the external borders through infrastructure and surveillance.	yes
然而，欧盟与各成员国就围栏费用支付等问题争吵不休。	However, the EU and member states continue to quarrel over issues such as payment of fence fees.	yes
冯德莱恩一再表示，欧盟资金不会支付相关费用。	Von der Leyen has stated time and again that EU funds will not pay the relevant expenses.	yes
但一些成员国的外交官员称，如果欧盟能分担外部边界沿线安装摄像头、瞭望塔和其他基础设施的部分，这将给各国腾出国家预算从而加快建设进程。	However, diplomats from some member states say that if the EU can share the part of installing cameras, observation towers, and other infrastructure along the external border, this will free up national budgets for countries and thus speed up the construction process.	yes
欧洲Euractiv网站称，欧盟官员承认，难民接收过程每一步都存在瓶颈，有限的接收能力和成员国不堪重负的移民当局无法阻止难民在欧盟各国提交“无数”庇护申请，欧盟的难民接收系统处于近乎“永久性的危机”中。	According to the European Euractiv website, EU officials acknowledge that there are bottlenecks at every step of the refugee reception process. Limited acceptance capacity and the overburdened immigration authorities of member states cannot prevent refugees from submitting “countless” asylum applications in EU countries, and that the EU refugee reception system is in an almost “permanent crisis.”	yes
据欧盟委员会估计，欧盟的申根国家去年收到超92万份庇护申请，比前一年增加近半。	According to European Commission estimates, EU Schengen countries received over 920,000 asylum applications last year, an increase of nearly half over the previous year.	yes

美国升级“芯片战”重创全球半导体产业-中新网	America's escalation of the “chip war” hits the global semiconductor industry-Sinomine.com	yes
最近，美国对华“芯片战”大有升级之势——先是荷兰、日本两国在美国施压下，同意启动对华半导体制造设备出口的管制；后有外媒报道，美国政府正考虑切断美国供应商与华为公司之间的所有联系，禁止美国供应商向华为提供任何产品；拜登政府还准备公布一项行政命令，限制美国对敏感的中国科技行业的投资……2023年开年不久，美国在遏制中国半导体相关产业发展上就恶招不断。	Recently, the US “chip war” against China has escalated — first, the Netherlands and Japan agreed to initiate controls on exports of semiconductor manufacturing equipment to China under pressure from the US; foreign media later reported that the US government was considering cutting off all ties between US suppliers and Huawei and prohibiting US suppliers from supplying any products to Huawei; the Biden administration is also preparing to issue an executive order restricting US investment in the sensitive Chinese technology industry... Shortly after the start of 2023, the US continued to make bad moves to curb the development of China's semiconductor-related industries.	yes
近年来，美国打击中国“芯”发展的动作从未停歇，一边精准打压对华半导体产供链，一边构建“去中国化”的半导体产业链联盟，图谋在先进半导体产业上彻底“甩开”中国。	In recent years, the US has never stopped cracking down on China's “core” development. While accurately suppressing the semiconductor production supply chain to China, it is building a “de-Chinesized” semiconductor industry chain alliance in an attempt to completely “throw out” China in the advanced semiconductor industry.	yes
无论是拉拢韩国建立“技术同盟”，还是与韩国、日本和中国台湾地区建立芯片“四方联盟”，亦或借由美日印澳“四边机制”“印太经济框架”等机制建立半导体产业链“小圈子”，美国通过把政治化、阵营化、武器化的手段引入半导体产业，企图搭建美国主导的封闭产供链循环，从而弥补其在芯片制造领域的短板，维护其在全球芯片产业的优势地位。	Whether it is winning over South Korea to establish a “technology alliance,” or establishing a “quadripartite alliance” for chips with South Korea, Japan, and Taiwan, or using mechanisms such as the “quadripartite mechanism” and “Indo-Pacific economic framework” between the US, Japan, India, and Australia, or the “Indo-Pacific Economic Framework” to establish a “small circle” in the semiconductor industry chain, the US has introduced politicized, camped, and weaponized means in an attempt to establish a closed production and supply chain cycle dominated by the US to make up for its shortcomings in the chip manufacturing field and maintain its dominant position in the global chip industry.	yes
然而，美国大张旗鼓的对华“芯战术”，也是“伤敌一千自损八百”。	However, America's “core tactic” against China with great fanfare is also “injuring 1,000 enemies and causing 800 self-damage.”	yes
最近，美国知名芯片制造设备供应商泛林集团宣布，受最新一轮对华芯片制造设备出口禁令影响，集团将解雇1300名全职员工，未来两个季度还计划解雇1400名临时员工。	Recently, Fanlin Group, a well-known American chip manufacturing equipment supplier, announced that due to the latest round of chip manufacturing equipment export bans to China, the group will lay off 1,300 full-time employees and plans to lay off 1,400 temporary employees in the next two quarters.	yes
全球光刻机巨头荷兰阿斯麦控股公司最近警告，禁止向中国出口半导体制造设备，可能导致半导体价格上涨。	The global lithography giant Dutch Asmarck Holding Company recently warned that a ban on the export of semiconductor manufacturing equipment to China could lead to a rise in semiconductor prices.	yes

美国所谓打压中国先进半导体产业，却把全球半导体产业链、供应链拖下了水。	America's so-called crackdown on China's advanced semiconductor industry has dragged down the global semiconductor industry chain and supply chain.	yes

据专业人士估算，基于专业化分工，半导体产品的整个生产过程需要跨越各国边境70次以上，全程达到100天。	According to expert estimates, based on a specialized division of labor, the entire production process of semiconductor products requires crossing the borders of various countries more than 70 times, reaching 100 days.	no

The minimum holding periods were 365 days, 540 days, 720 days, and 1080 days, respectively. 《办法》规定，参加人可以通过个人养老金资金账户购买个人养老储蓄、个人养老金理财产品、个人养老金保险产品、个人养老金公募基金产品等个人养老金产品。	The “Measures” stipulate that participants can purchase personal pension products such as personal pension savings, personal pension wealth management products, personal pension insurance products, and personal pension public fund products through personal pension fund accounts.	no
随后，人社部、财政部、国家税务总局三部门发布通知，明确个人养老金制度在北京、天津，以及河北石家庄、雄安新区，山西晋城市等36个先行城市和地区启动实施。	Subsequently, the three departments of the Ministry of Human Resources and Social Affairs, the Ministry of Finance, and the State Administration of Taxation issued notices clarifying that the personal pension system will be implemented in Beijing, Tianjin, and 36 pioneering cities and regions, including Shijiazhuang and Xiong'an New District in Hebei, and Jincheng in Shanxi.	no
截至2022年底，个人养老金参加人数1954万人，缴费人数613万人，总缴费金额142亿元。	By the end of 2022, the number of individual pension participants was 19.54 million, and the number of contributors was 6.13 million, with a total contribution amount of 14.2 billion yuan.	no

如今，个人养老金理财产品也聚齐之后，投资者该如何选择？	Now that personal pension wealth management products are also available, how should investors choose?	no
交银理财产品研发部专家表示，相比其他个人养老金产品，试点阶段的养老理财产品和个人养老金理财产品均具有三方面的特点。	Experts from the BOCOM Wealth Management Product Research and Development Department said that compared to other personal pension products, the pilot phase of the pension wealth management products and personal pension wealth management products all have three characteristics.	no
一是稳健性，风险管理机制更加健全，投资策略和理念更为稳健，并实施非母行第三方独立托管。	The first is prudence. The risk management mechanism is more complete, investment strategies and ideas are more stable, and independent hosting is implemented by a third party other than the parent bank.	no
二是长期性，试点阶段养老理财产品的期限都在5年及以上，下一步发行的个人养老金理财产品，最短持有期原则上为1年，鼓励持有3年以上。	Second, they are long-term. The term of all pension wealth management products in the pilot phase is 5 years or more. The minimum holding period for personal pension wealth management products to be issued in the next step is 1 year in principle, and holdings of at least 3 years are encouraged.	no
三是普惠性，产品购买门槛低，起购点一般为1元，有的低至0.01元，产品的托管费、管理费等费率更加优惠。	Third, inclusiveness. The purchase threshold for products is low. The starting point of purchase is generally 1 yuan, and some are as low as 0.01 yuan. The rates for product hosting fees, management fees, etc. are even more favorable.	no
专业人士指出，投资者要根据产品特点和自己的风险承受能力进行选择。	Experts pointed out that investors should choose according to product characteristics and their risk tolerance.	no
个人养老金储蓄具有期限较长、利率较高、安全性高的特点，适合风险承受能力弱的人群；个人养老金保险产品重在保障，比较适合无法承担投资风险，可以接受稳定收益的人群；而个人养老金理财产品和公募基金产品不保本也不保收益，有一定投资风险，但预期收益较高，适合具备一定的金融知识、风险承担能力较高的人群。	Personal pension savings have the characteristics of long terms, high interest rates, and high safety, and are suitable for people with poor risk tolerance; personal pension insurance products focus on protection and are more suitable for people who cannot bear investment risks and can accept stable returns; while personal pension wealth management products and public fund products do not protect capital or income, have certain investment risks, but the expected returns are high, suitable for people with certain financial knowledge and high risk bearing ability.	no
文/本报记者 程婕 统筹/池海波	Text/Co-ordinated by Cheng Jie, reporter of this newspaper/Chi Haibo	no
健身行业应摆脱信任危机-中新网	The fitness industry should get rid of the crisis of trust-Sinomine.com	yes
又一大型健身房“暴雷”？	Another big gym “thunderstorm”?	yes
近日，知名健身机构中健健身会员维权问题引起社会关注。	Recently, the issue of rights protection for members of Zhongjian Fitness, a well-known fitness institution, attracted public attention.	yes
春节后不少会员发现自己所在门店没有正常营业，随后，关于该机构倒闭跑路的传闻引起会员恐慌，导致公安、人社部门介入。	After the Spring Festival, many members discovered that their stores were not operating normally. Afterwards, rumors about the agency going out of business caused members to panic, causing public security and social affairs departments to intervene.	yes
最后，该机构相关负责人出面回应，承诺会努力保障好员工和会员的合法权益，风波才得以平息。	Finally, the relevant person in charge of the agency came forward to respond, promising that efforts would be made to protect the legitimate rights and interests of employees and members before the storm was brought to an end.	yes
个别健身机构的部分门店出现经营问题，暂时关闭，消费者本可心平气和等待问题解决，为何不少会员的第一反应是“大事不妙”？	Some stores of individual fitness institutions have had business problems and are temporarily closed. Consumers could have been calm and wait for the problem to be solved. Why is the first reaction of so many members “big things not good”?	yes
健身俱乐部会员维权风波背后，是行业信任危机的深层次问题。	Behind the fitness club members' rights protection storm is the deep-seated issue of the industry's trust crisis.	yes
国内传统健身房普遍采取预付费模式，“赚用户不来的钱”是其发展的底层逻辑。	Traditional gyms in China generally adopt a prepaid model, and “making money users don't get” is the underlying logic of their development.	yes
通过预售会员卡获取现金流，不断开新店，看似能够循环往复，实则寅吃卯粮，无法形成稳定的盈利模式。	Obtaining cash flow through pre-selling membership cards and continuously opening new stores seems to be able to cycle back and forth. In fact, Yin eats food and is unable to form a stable profit model.	yes
健身房跑路等行业负面信息频频传出，对消费者信心造成强烈冲击。	Negative information from gyms and other industries is frequently coming out, which has had a strong impact on consumer confidence.	yes
从市场前景看，健身房当然算得上是一门有“钱途”的好生意。	Judging from market prospects, gyms can of course be considered a good business with “money.”	no
健身赛道虽然起起伏伏，但始终受到资本关注。	Despite the ups and downs of fitness tracks, they have always received capital attention.	no
多项数据显示，文体消费等领域热度不断攀升，市场持续回暖。	According to various data, the popularity of fields such as cultural and sports consumption continues to rise, and the market continues to pick up.	no
具体到健身市场，随着居民生活水平稳步提高，健康生活理念深入人心，健身行业发展大有可为。	Specifically with regard to the fitness market, with the steady improvement of residents' living standards and the concept of a healthy lifestyle, the fitness industry has great potential for development.	no
形势越是趋好，行业越需重视发展质量。	The better the situation, the more the industry needs to pay attention to the quality of development.	no
然而，个别机构对消费复苏后的健身市场盲目乐观，刚从危机中走出来，又吹响开疆拓土的号角，把融资资金一股脑投入新店建设上。	However, some institutions are blindly optimistic about the fitness market after consumption has recovered. Having just emerged from the crisis, they are also sounding the trumpet of opening up land, investing all of their financing funds into the construction of new stores.	no
不可否认，这几年受疫情影响，不少机构退出，行业重新洗牌，有实力的企业此时选择性地加大收购力度、重新布局，未尝不是新机遇。	It is undeniable that due to the impact of the epidemic in recent years, many institutions have withdrawn, and the industry has been reshuffled. At this time, powerful enterprises have selectively stepped up their acquisition efforts and restructured. Failure to explore this is not a new opportunity.	no
但是，健身市场发展要想进入良性循环，迈上行稳致远的康庄大道，行业就必须改变传统模式，改变经营策略。	However, if the fitness market is to enter a virtuous cycle and embark on the steady and far-reaching Kangzhuang Avenue, the industry must change its traditional model and business strategy.	no
只有稳扎稳打，重新建立起消费者的信任度、安全感，才能真正赢得市场、赢得未来。	Only by working steadily and re-establishing consumers' trust and sense of security can we truly win the market and win the future.	no
相比大建新店抢占市场，健身行业当前更需要的是沉下心来优化服务，用高质量发展来稳住用户。	Compared to building a new store to seize the market, what the fitness industry currently needs more is to calm down to optimize services and use high-quality development to stabilize users.	no
首先，要靠服务留住用户。	First, it's up to the service to retain users.	no
健身房属于服务行业，其本质是坚持“用户导向”，要紧紧围绕用户需求，把经营重心放在服务提质升级上。	Gyms belong to the service industry. Their essence is to adhere to “user orientation”, focus closely on user needs, and focus operations on improving service quality and upgrading.	no
其次，要靠数字化转型提升用户体验。	Second, it is up to digital transformation to improve the user experience.	no
比如当下流行的互联网健身房模式，实现用户按次付费和场地自选。	For example, the current popular internet gym model allows users to pay per time and choose the venue.	no
同时，身体数据、运动数据得以有效利用，还可以满足社交需求，实现从线上到线下完整的服务闭环。	At the same time, physical data and exercise data can be effectively utilized to meet social needs and achieve a closed loop of complete services from online to offline.	no
没有私教推销，没有巨额年卡，用户对健身机构“跑路”的担忧降低了，信任感也就提升了。	Without private education promotions and huge annual passes, users' concerns about fitness institutions “running” have been reduced, and their sense of trust has also increased.	no
另外，还要积极探索多元业态。	Furthermore, it is also necessary to actively explore diverse business formats.	no
如今，体育消费已经从单一服务走向场景消费，健身俱乐部有望成为消费新入口，围绕健身所需的运动补给和健身器械等周边产品或将成为新的盈利点，为消费者提供更丰富选择。	Nowadays, sports consumption has moved from a single service to scenario consumption, and fitness clubs are expected to become new consumers. Peripheral products such as exercise supplements and fitness equipment required for fitness may become new profit points, providing consumers with richer choices.	no

买贵退差价！	Buy more and get back the difference!	yes
南京楼市再现“差价赔付”-中新网	Nanjing property market reproduces “price difference compensation” -Sinomine.com	yes
扬子晚报讯(记者 马祚波)扬子晚报/紫牛新闻记者10日在采访中发现，十余年未见的“保价协议”又重回了南京楼市，位于江北新区的一家楼盘宣称“差价赔付”，在交房前其他房源的优惠大于之前的折扣，开发商愿意为买房人换房并退还差价。	Yangzi Evening News (Reporter Ma Zuobo) The Yangzi Evening News/Ziniu News reporter discovered in an interview on the 10th that the “insurance price agreement” that had not been seen in more than 10 years had returned to the Nanjing property market. A property located in the Jiangbei New Area claimed “price difference compensation.” The discount on other properties was greater than the previous discount before the house was handed over, and the developers were willing to exchange and refund the difference in price for the buyer.	yes
“保价协议”条件可不少	There are quite a few “insurance agreement” conditions	yes
这家位于江北新区的楼盘名为保利扬子萃云台，看房人孙先生告诉记者，他在上周末逛楼盘时发现了一则“声明”。	The name of this property in the Jiangbei New Area is Poly Yangzi Cuiyuntai. The housekeeper, Mr. Sun, told the reporter that he discovered a “statement” while visiting the property last weekend.	yes
他发给记者的图片上显示，该楼盘的开发商承诺，凡是在2月1日-2月28日期间购买房源的，自双方签订买卖合同之日起至对应房源交付，若该项目其他房源的优惠折扣大于之前购房所享折扣的(限与该商品房属于同一户型、同一楼栋、同一单元、同一物业类型的其他未售商品房)，开发商可以为购房者换房并退还差价。	The picture he sent to the reporter showed that the developer of the property promised that anyone who purchased the property between February 1 and February 28 from the date the two parties signed the purchase and sale contract until the delivery of the corresponding property, if the preferential discount for other properties in the project is greater than the discount previously enjoyed by the purchase of the house (limited to other unsold commercial properties of the same type, same building, same unit, and same property type as the commercial property), the developer can exchange the house for the buyer and refund the difference in price.	yes
孙先生表示，置业顾问表示这其实就是一份“保价协议”，目的是让买家放心出手，不用担心开发企业降价促销，“现在就怕买完了它就降价了，去售楼处闹吧没时间，不闹的话也确实窝心”。	Mr. Sun said that the real estate consultant said that this is actually an “insured price agreement”. The purpose is to reassure the buyer and not worry about the development company's price reduction promotion. “Now I'm afraid that the price will drop once I've bought it. There's no time to go to the sales office; if you don't make a fuss, I'm really worried.”	yes
还有不少买房人则认为，“保价协议”虽然是在给购房者吃“定心丸”，不过条件却不低。	There are also quite a few buyers who think that although the “insurance price agreement” is a “reassurance pill” for buyers, the conditions are not low.	yes
打算在江北买一套刚需房的郑女士说，保价的房源首先是要同一户型，还得在同一楼栋、同一个单元，买家可以比价的房源寥寥，因此“门槛”还是蛮高的。	Ms. Zheng, who is planning to buy a house she just needed in Jiangbei, said that the first thing to insured property is to have the same apartment type; it also has to be in the same building and unit. There are few properties that buyers can compare prices, so the “threshold” is still quite high.	yes
也有购房者认为，由于信息不对称，销售时不排除给出额外的让利，买家“维权”的难度不小。	There are also buyers who think that due to asymmetric information and additional concessions are not ruled out when selling, it is not too difficult for buyers to “defend their rights.”	yes
能否留住买房人有待观察	Whether it can keep buyers remains to be seen	no
记者在南京网上房地产上查询得知，该楼盘于去年11月首领两幢楼共计252套房源的销许，户型面积有105平方米、114平方米、129平方米等，全装修销许均价为39843元/㎡。	The reporter inquired online real estate in Nanjing and learned that in November of last year, the property led the sale of a total of 252 units in the two buildings. The apartment area was 105 square meters, 114 square meters, 129 square meters, etc., and the average price of the fully furnished license was 39,843 yuan/㎡.	no
不过两个多月过去，网上房地产显示目前该楼盘的未售总套数为157套，占比为62.3%，其中8号楼共计128套，未售套数达113套，7号楼的124套中也有44套未售，项目的总成交套数只有33套，占比仅为13%。	However, more than two months have passed, and online real estate shows that the total number of unsold units in this property is currently 157, accounting for 62.3%. Of these, Building 8 has a total of 128 units, and the number of unsold units has reached 113. Of the 124 units in Building 7, 44 units are also unsold. The total number of units sold for the project is only 33, accounting for only 13%.	no
市场人士介绍，“保价协议”在2008年也曾在南京出现过。	According to market sources, “insurance price agreements” also appeared in Nanjing in 2008.	no
当年8月份，河西黄山路上的楼盘横塘西苑为了吸引买房人眼球，推出了《保价计划》，具体内容为“公司郑重承诺，若一年内项目优惠幅度扩大，由此产生的差额，公司将按差额退还给老业主”。	In August of that year, in order to attract the attention of buyers, Hengtang Xiyuan, a real estate on Huangshan Road in Hexi, launched the “Price Insurance Plan”. The details were “The company solemnly promises that if the project discount margin expands within one year, the difference resulting from this will be refunded to the old owners.”	no
此后2011年4月，南京也有9家楼盘拿出部分房源承诺“差价赔付”。	Since then, in 2011/4, 9 properties in Nanjing also offered part of their listings and promised to “pay the difference in price.”	no
“楼市在回暖，此时更需要一针‘强心剂’。	“The property market is picking up, and a 'strength agent' is needed even more at this time.	no
”南京地产行业一位资深操盘手沈先生表示，“保价协议”也是房企的营销方式之一。	Mr. Shen, a senior trader in the Nanjing real estate industry, said that “insured price agreements” are also one of the marketing methods for housing enterprises.	no
他认为如今开发企业比买房人更需要信心，推出“保价协议”其实也是在给其打气。	He believes that development companies now need more confidence than buyers; the introduction of an “insured price agreement” is actually encouraging them.	no
至于能否留住买房人，他表示这取决于调控政策、贷款门槛等多重因素的影响，就目前来看仍有待观察。	As to whether buyers can be retained, he said that this depends on the influence of multiple factors such as regulatory policies and loan thresholds, so it remains to be seen.	no

新华社台北2月11日电(记者赵博、黄扬)出口贸易额“连五黑”，制造业采购经理人指数(PMI)连续7个月紧缩，消费者物价指数(CPI)又见“3字头”……近期，台湾当局陆续发布2023年1月经济数据。	Xinhua News Agency report of February 11 from Taipei (by staff reporters Zhao Bo and Huang Yang) - Export trade volume has been “in a row”, the manufacturing purchasing managers' index (PMI) has been tightening for 7 consecutive months, and the consumer price index (CPI) has also seen “3 letters”... 据台当局财政事务主管部门公布，台湾地区今年1月出口315.1亿美元，年减21.2%，连续第5个月负增长。	According to an announcement from the financial affairs department of the Taiwan authorities, Taiwan exported 31.51 billion US dollars in January this year, a decrease of 21.2% per year, for the 5th consecutive month of negative growth.	yes

该部门统计处长蔡美娜表示，这显示消费性电子产业需求疲弱效应扩散，电子产业进入修正期。	The department's statistics director, Choi Mei Na, said that this shows that the effects of weak demand in the consumer electronics industry are spreading, and that the electronics industry has entered a correction period.	yes

经济监测指标体系中，PMI以50%为荣枯线，指数大于50%，代表景气扩张，反之为紧缩。	In the economic monitoring index system, the PMI uses 50% as the boom and bust line, and the index is greater than 50%, representing economic expansion, and conversely, contraction.	no

其中，蔬菜价格飞涨28.25%，创17个月新高。	Among them, vegetable prices soared 28.25% to a 17-month high.	no

2022年回国求职应届留学生留学国前10 图源：《2022中国海归就业调查报告》	Top 10 Job Seeking Students Studying Abroad in 2022 Source: “2022 China Overseas Returnees Employment Survey Report”	yes
中新网北京2月11日电 (门睿)近日发布的《2022中国海归就业调查报告》(下称“报告”)显示，2022年应届留学生规模同比增长8.6%，回国求职留学生数量再创新高，我国企业对海外人才的需求亦呈上扬态势。	China News Network, Beijing, Feb. 11 (Men Rui) The “2022 China Overseas Returnees Employment Survey Report” (hereinafter referred to as the “Report”) recently released shows that the number of fresh international students in 2022 increased by 8.6% year on year, the number of students returning home to seek employment reached a new high, and the demand for overseas talents from Chinese enterprises is also on the rise.	yes
报告指出，自2020年以来，在中国国内求职的海归数量明显增长，回国求职的应届留学生数量增多。	The report points out that since 2020, the number of overseas returnees seeking employment in China has increased markedly, and the number of fresh students returning home to seek employment has increased.	yes
与2021年相比，2022年应届留学生规模同比增长8.6%，回国求职留学生数量再创新高。	Compared with 2021, the number of fresh international students in 2022 increased by 8.6% year on year, and the number of students returning home to seek employment reached a new high.	yes
从回国求职留学生的留学国家分布来看，英国占比最高，为41.4%，其次是澳大利亚(20.3%)和美国(9%)，排名与2021年一致。	Judging from the distribution of study abroad countries for returning to work, the UK accounted for the highest proportion, at 41.4%, followed by Australia (20.3%) and the US (9%), which are in line with 2021.	yes
从同比增速来看，2022年来自马来西亚、日本、新加坡的应届留学生人数同比大幅上升，增速分别为66.1%、50.9%和37.7%。	Looking at the year-on-year growth rate, the number of fresh international students from Malaysia, Japan, and Singapore rose sharply year on year in 2022, with growth rates of 66.1%, 50.9%, and 37.7%, respectively.	yes
来自加拿大、德国、美国、澳大利亚的应届留学生人数同比下降。	The number of fresh students from Canada, Germany, the US, and Australia declined year over year.	yes

央视网消息：种植牙是很多缺牙患者的理想选择，但一直以来，动辄上万元一颗的价格让很多患者望而却步。	CCTV News: Dental implants are an ideal choice for many patients with missing teeth, but the price of each tooth has always discouraged many patients.	yes
今年以来，随着种植牙集采的加速落地，各地也将种植牙降价提上日程。	Since this year, with the accelerated implementation of dental implant collection, various regions have also put dental implant price reductions on the agenda.	yes
从2月10日起，河南省单颗常规种植牙医疗服务价格全流程调控目标为4300元，单颗常规种植全流程费用不高于调控目标的97%。	Starting February 10, the price of a single conventional dental implant medical service in Henan Province is 4,300 yuan, and the cost of the whole process of a single routine dental implant is not higher than 97% of the regulation target.	yes
种植牙齿指的是一种以植入骨组织内的下部结构为基础来支持、固位上部牙修复体的缺牙修复方式。	Dental implants refer to a missing tooth repair method that supports and fixes the upper tooth restoration body based on a lower structure implanted in bone tissue.	yes
记者从郑州大学第一附属医院了解到，以单颗常规种植为例，从种植到最后修复，价格大概要一万六七千元左右。	The reporter learned from the First Affiliated Hospital of Zhengzhou University that, taking a single routine implant as an example, the price from implantation to final restoration is roughly 167,000 yuan.	yes
患者 何莹：新政策之后，大夫跟我说，像我这种情况差不多就是8000多元、不到1万元，基本上能省一半。	Patient He Ying: After the new policy, the doctor told me that in my situation it was about 8,000 yuan, less than 10,000 yuan, which is basically half the savings.	yes
在现行项目基础上，河南省还整合确定了“种植体植入费(单颗)”等15个口腔种植类医疗服务价格项目，并统一制定省管公立医疗机构价格和医保支付类别，取消或调整了牙种植体植入术等20个医疗服务价格项目。	On the basis of current projects, Henan Province has also integrated and determined 15 dental implant medical service price items, including “implant implants (single tablet),” uniformly formulated prices and medical insurance payment categories for public medical institutions managed by the province, and cancelled or adjusted 20 medical service price items such as dental implant implants.	yes
郑州市医疗保障局医药价格和招标采购处处长 李云杰：受益的主要是四方，一个是医保，医保的支出少了；医院的占压少了，病人会适当增加；对供应商来说得到了一个市场；对我们患者来说是得利最大的一方，植一颗牙的费用可能要减半甚至更多。	Li Yunjie, Director of the Pharmaceutical Prices and Bidding and Procurement Department of the Zhengzhou Municipal Medical Security Bureau: The main beneficiaries are medical insurance; medical insurance expenses are less; patients will increase appropriately when the pressure on hospitals is less; suppliers get a market; for our patients, it is the side that benefits the most; for our patients, the cost of implanting a tooth may have to be halved or even more.	yes

中新网2月11日电 题：中国电商行业涌现“新变量”，带货如何做到“内容为王”？	China News Network, Feb. 11: “New variables” have emerged in China's e-commerce industry. How can delivery achieve “content is king”?	yes
