“我们入局电商算是晚的，但从最开始就意识到，想要从千千万万的店铺中脱颖而出，内容很重要。	“It was too late for us to enter e-commerce, but we realized from the beginning that if we want to stand out from the tens of millions of stores, content is important.	yes
”来自广东的“90后”女生芳芳，现在在抖音电商运营一家滋补食材店铺，让一家有着30多年历史的线下店在线上“开花”。	” Fang Fang, a “post-90s” girl from Guangdong, now runs a nutritional food store on Douyin e-commerce, making an offline store with a history of more than 30 years “blossom” online.	yes
模仿老港片影调、配上经典粤语歌，打开@芳芳一人食抖音账号，精美的视频令人耳目一新。	Imitating the tunes of old Hong Kong movies with classic Cantonese songs, open @芳芳一人食抖音账号. The beautiful videos are refreshing.	yes
在近日举行的抖音电商“寻找同行者·优质内容分享专场”上，芳芳作为优质创作者代表到场发言，介绍了日常创作的经历和体会。	At the Douyin e-commerce “Find Peers · Quality Content Sharing Session” held recently, Fang Fang spoke as a representative of quality creators and introduced her daily creative experiences and experiences.	yes
她在现场说：“精心打磨的视频收获了很多网友的关注，好多人对我家的食材感兴趣，想跟着一起做美食，销路就一下子打开了。	She said on the scene, “The carefully polished video has garnered a lot of attention from netizens. Many people are interested in our ingredients and want to cook food with them, and sales channels have opened up all of a sudden.	yes
”	”	yes
芳芳靠着煲汤视频让更多人爱上“老广的味道”，一场直播最多卖出30万件滋补食材，挽救了家里濒临倒闭的老店。	Fang Fang relied on the soup cooking video to make more people fall in love with the “taste of old people”. A live broadcast sold up to 300,000 pieces of nutritional ingredients, saving his family's old store that was on the verge of going out of business.	no
“无内容，不电商”，随着短视频和直播电商不断发展，人们对电商内容的要求和标准正步入新阶段。	“No content, no e-commerce”. With the continuous development of short video and live e-commerce, people's requirements and standards for e-commerce content are entering a new stage.	no
直播带货发展初期，直播间往往用低价折扣吸引用户，价格优势似乎成了当时的唯一卖点。	In the early days of live streaming delivery, live broadcast rooms often used low price discounts to attract users, and the price advantage seemed to be the only selling point at the time.	no
近年来，既有刘畊宏、东方甄选等现象级大V，也有在垂直细分领域出现的不少非大众所知的达人和商家，他们通过持续打造符合自己品牌调性的优质内容，提升长期经营效益。	In recent years, there have been phenomenal figures such as Liu Yihong and Oriental Selection, as well as many unwell-known experts and merchants that have emerged in vertical segments. They have enhanced long-term business efficiency by continuously creating high-quality content that matches their brand tone.	no
抖音电商明星作者运营负责人高亚轩介绍，过去一年有627万创作者通过抖音电商将内容变现，他们的内容创作量增长了252%，总成交额也翻了一倍以上。	Gao Yaxuan, head of operation of Douyin E-Commerce Star Author, explained that in the past year, 6.27 million creators have monetized content through Douyin e-commerce. Their content creation volume has increased by 252%, and the total turnover has more than doubled.	no
“在这些数字背后，我们能感受到一个蓬勃生长、具有旺盛生命力的作者生态。	“Behind these numbers, we can feel a thriving, vibrant author ecosystem.	no
”高亚轩说。	” Gao Yaxuan said.	no
北京师范大学传播创新与未来媒体实验平台此前发布了《电商行业内容生态健康指数(ECHI)报告》，从数据维度解析了当前电商行业中“新变量”——优质内容的重要性，运用指数对国内27家主流电商平台内容生态情况进行了评估。	The Communication Innovation and Future Media Experimental Platform of Beijing Normal University previously released the “E-commerce Industry Content Ecological Health Index (ECHI) Report”, which analyzed the “new variable” in the current e-commerce industry — the importance of high-quality content — from a data perspective, and used the index to evaluate the content ecology of 27 mainstream e-commerce platforms in China.	no
根据上述报告的电商行业内容生态健康指数排名，抖音电商、快手、淘宝、拼多多、京东位居前五。	According to the e-commerce industry content ecological health index ranking of the above report, Douyin e-commerce, Kuaishou, Taobao, Pinduoduo, and Jingdong rank in the top five.	no
报告认为，电商行业内容生态是一个综合性概念，是将电商与内容进行整合，但并非所有内容都可与电商整合，好的PGC(专业生产内容)与UGC(用户原创内容)才是与电商进行整合的优质载体，内容平台价值越高，消费与推广的场景也就越来越丰富，电商植入的可能性也就越高，商业价值也就越强，这种公共领域和私人领域逐步集成分布的电商内容生产和内容消费的比例也就会越高。	According to the report, the e-commerce industry's content ecosystem is a comprehensive concept that integrates e-commerce with content, but not all content can be integrated with e-commerce. Good PGC (professional production content) and UGC (user original content) are high-quality carriers for integration with e-commerce. The higher the value of the content platform, the richer the consumption and promotion scenarios, the higher the possibility of e-commerce implantation, and the stronger the commercial value.	no
现场，北京师范大学新闻传播学院教授、中国传媒经济与管理专业委员会理事长喻国明对《报告》做了分析解读。	On the scene, Yu Guoming, a professor at the School of Journalism and Communication at Beijing Normal University and chairman of the China Media Economics and Management Committee, gave an analysis and interpretation of the “Report.”	no
他表示，就内容价值而言，当前电商行业已经从“消费可及性”过渡到“消费品质化”阶段，优质、专业、差异化的内容是电商行业的“硬通货”。	He said that as far as content value is concerned, the e-commerce industry has now transitioned from “consumption accessibility” to the “consumption quality” stage. High-quality, professional, and differentiated content is the “hard currency” of the e-commerce industry.	no
同时，内容成为电商发展新阶段的根本和抓手，知识付费、专业性知识、KOL(关键意见领袖)等PGC内容开始在电商直播中成为标配。	At the same time, content has become the foundation and starting point of the new stage of e-commerce development, and PGC content such as knowledge payments, professional knowledge, and KOLs (key opinion leaders) are beginning to become standard in e-commerce live broadcasts.	no
展望电商行业的未来发展，喻国明提出两方面的建议。	Looking forward to the future development of the e-commerce industry, Yu Guoming put forward two suggestions.	no
一个是从内容结构提升的角度看，推动电商内容生态健康程度和质量整体提升，打造正向内容创作和管理标准，实现电商行业内容生态健康系统指数与动态均衡。	One is to promote the overall improvement of the ecological health and quality of e-commerce content from the perspective of improving the content structure, establish positive content creation and management standards, and achieve a balance between the e-commerce industry's content ecological health system index and dynamics.	no
另一个是从外部生态看，要实现内容电商行业的健康发展和外部环境的价值协同与共创。	The other is that from the perspective of the external ecology, it is necessary to achieve the healthy development of the content e-commerce industry and value collaboration and co-creation of the external environment.	no
“未来电商行业还需要更多的数据、人工智能方面的支持，形成对未来发展稳定性的预测；此外，为商家提供更规范、健康的成长空间，实现电商行业中企业、用户、产品与服务的价值协同，共创健康内容生态。	“The future e-commerce industry also needs more data and artificial intelligence support to predict future development stability; in addition, it provides merchants with a more standardized and healthy growth space, realizes value synergy between enterprises, users, products and services in the e-commerce industry, and co-creates a healthy content ecosystem.	no
”(完)	” (complete)	no
北交所融资融券交易业务下周启动-中新网	The financing and securities trading business of the Beijing Stock Exchange will start next week.-Sinomine.com	yes
本报讯(记者 孙杰)昨晚，北交所发布消息，经中国证监会批准，北京证券交易所融资融券交易业务将于2月13日正式启动，届时已取得北交所融资融券交易权限的证券公司可接受投资者委托，向北交所进行融资融券交易申报。	News from this newspaper (Reporter Sun Jie) Last night, the Beijing Stock Exchange released news that with the approval of the China Securities Regulatory Commission, the financing and securities trading business of the Beijing Stock Exchange will be officially launched on February 13. At that time, securities companies that have obtained the Beijing Stock Exchange's securities financing transaction authority can accept requests from investors to report financing and securities transactions to the Beijing Stock Exchange.	yes
首批56只融资融券标的股票名单以2023年1月31日为计算基准日确定。	The list of the first batch of 56 securities financing stocks was determined using January 31, 2023 as the calculation base date.	yes
北交所表示，融资融券标的股票名单和可充抵保证金证券名单将通过北交所官网的“信息披露-融资融券信息”栏目公布，方便投资者查询。	The Beijing Stock Exchange said that the list of stocks covered by securities financing and the list of securities that can be used as security deposits will be published through the “Information Disclosure - Securities Finance Information” section of the Beijing Stock Exchange's official website to facilitate investors' inquiries.	yes
融资融券是证券市场重要的基础性制度，也是国际证券市场中较为成熟的交易方式。	Securities financing is an important basic system in the securities market, and it is also a more mature transaction method in the international securities market.	yes
去年9月2日，在宣布设立一周年之际，北交所对融资融券业务公开征求意见。	On September 2 of last year, on the occasion of announcing the first anniversary of its establishment, the Beijing Stock Exchange solicited public comments on securities financing and securities lending business.	yes
北交所融资融券交易的启动是持续推进北交所市场制度建设、完善交易机制、提升二级市场定价功能的重要举措。	The launch of securities financing transactions on the Beijing Stock Exchange is an important measure to continue to promote the Beijing Stock Exchange's market system construction, improve the trading mechanism, and enhance the pricing function of the secondary market.	yes
融资融券制度有利于丰富投资者交易策略，满足投资者多元交易需求，促进市场价格发现，进一步提升市场流动性。	The securities financing system is conducive to enriching investors' trading strategies, meeting investors' diversified trading needs, promoting market price discovery, and further enhancing market liquidity.	yes
下一步，北交所将在中国证监会的领导下，持续做好融资融券业务各项保障工作，以投资者需求为导向丰富交易制度工具，完善相关配套机制，着力打造服务创新型中小企业的一流交易所。	In the next step, under the leadership of the China Securities Regulatory Commission, the Beijing Stock Exchange will continue to do a good job of safeguarding the financing and securities lending business, enrich trading system tools guided by investors' needs, improve relevant supporting mechanisms, and focus on building a first-class exchange serving innovative small and medium-sized enterprises.	yes

中国救援队在土耳其持续开展救援行动 已营救4名被困人员-中新网	The Chinese rescue team continues to carry out rescue operations in Turkey and has rescued 4 trapped persons-Sinomine.com	yes
中新网2月11日电 据应急管理部网站11日消息，2月10日，正在土耳其搜救的中国救援队派出3个行动分队、45名救援队员，营救出1名被困人员。	China News Network, Feb. 11 - According to information on the Ministry of Emergency Management's website on the 11th, the Chinese rescue team currently searching and rescuing Turkey dispatched 3 operation detachments and 45 rescue team members to rescue 1 trapped person.	yes
同时派出2个搜索评估组，对沃达巴什大街15栋建筑进行评估排查。	At the same time, 2 search and evaluation teams were dispatched to evaluate and investigate 15 buildings on Vodabash Street.	yes
截至目前，共营救4名被困人员，搜寻出5名遇难者，对25栋倒塌严重的建筑进行生命迹象和风险评估。	Up to now, a total of 4 trapped people have been rescued, 5 victims have been located, and vital signs and risk assessments have been carried out on 25 seriously collapsed buildings.	yes
救援队将根据灾区实际和救援现场情况，科学调整救援力量，持续深入开展救援工作。	The rescue team will scientifically adjust the rescue force according to the actual situation in the disaster area and the rescue site, and continue to carry out in-depth rescue work.	yes
救援队通过使馆、当地政府、联合国救援组织等多种渠道获取救援求助信息，通过线上询情、现场搜索等多种方式进行逐一核实。	The rescue team obtains rescue request information through various channels such as embassies, local governments, and United Nations rescue organizations, and verifies them one by one through various methods such as online inquiries and on-site searches.	yes
向中国香港救援队介绍目前救援环境和建筑坍塌等情况，联合开展搜索行动。	The Hong Kong rescue team was briefed on the current rescue environment and the collapse of buildings, etc., and jointly carried out a search operation.	yes
目前与意大利救援队联合负责区域协调(SSC5)，同时派遣3名队员参加5号区域救援协调中心工作，与意大利、英国、塞尔维亚、斯洛伐克、阿曼等多支队伍进行沟通，了解了联合国救援组织和各国救援队救援工作情况。	Currently, they are jointly responsible for regional coordination (SSC5) with the Italian rescue team. At the same time, 3 team members have been dispatched to work at Regional Rescue Coordination Center No. 5. 救援队持续强化安全管理和队伍保障，按照“统一指挥、安全第一”原则，加强救援现场安全管控，强化救援工作纪律要求，明确安全注意事项。	The rescue team continues to strengthen safety management and team security, strengthen safety control at rescue sites, strengthen disciplinary requirements for rescue work, and clarify safety precautions in accordance with the principle of “unified command, safety first”.	yes
持续运行轮值备勤和岗哨工作制度，强化营区安全管理。	Continue to operate the rotational duty preparation and guard duty work system to strengthen camp safety management.	yes

新华社北京2月11日电 题：推进中国式现代化是一个系统工程——四论深刻领会习近平总书记在学习贯彻党的二十大精神研讨班开班式重要讲话	Xinhua News Agency report of February 11 from Beijing: Promoting Chinese-style modernization is a systematic project - Four discussions on deeply understanding General Secretary Xi Jinping's important speech at the opening ceremony of the seminar on studying and implementing the spirit of the 20th National Congress of the Party	yes
新华社评论员	Commentator of Xinhua News Agency	yes
“推进中国式现代化是一个系统工程，需要统筹兼顾、系统谋划、整体推进，正确处理好顶层设计与实践探索、战略与策略、守正与创新、效率与公平、活力与秩序、自立自强与对外开放等一系列重大关系。	“Promoting Chinese-style modernization is a systematic project that requires an integrated approach, systematic planning, and overall promotion to properly handle a series of major relationships between top-level design and practical exploration, strategy and strategy, integrity and innovation, efficiency and fairness, vitality and order, self-reliance and self-improvement, and openness to the outside world.	yes
”在新进中央委员会的委员、候补委员和省部级主要领导干部学习贯彻习近平新时代中国特色社会主义思想和党的二十大精神研讨班开班式上，习近平总书记科学把握现代化建设规律，深入系统阐明实践中需要处理好的一系列重大关系，为我们大力推进中国式现代化提供了科学方法论。	” At the opening ceremony of the seminar for new members of the Central Committee, alternate members and leading cadres at the provincial ministry level to study and implement Xi Jinping's ideology of socialism with Chinese characteristics in the new era and the spirit of the 20th National Congress of the Party, General Secretary Xi Jinping scientifically grasped the rules of modernization and thoroughly and systematically clarified a series of major relationships that need to be handled in practice, providing us with a scientific methodology for vigorously advancing Chinese-style modernization.	yes
推进中国式现代化涉及经济、政治、文化、社会、生态文明等各个领域，关系治党治国治军、内政外交国防等方方面面，既要做好系统谋划，又要勇于改革创新，不断实现整体推进。	Promoting Chinese-style modernization involves various fields such as the economy, politics, culture, society, and ecological civilization. It is related to all aspects of governing the Party, the country, and the military, internal affairs, diplomacy, and national defense. It is necessary not only to do a good job in systematic planning, but also to be brave in reform and innovation to continuously achieve overall progress.	yes
进行顶层设计，需要深刻洞察世界发展大势，准确把握人民群众的共同愿望，深入探索经济社会发展规律，使制定的规划和政策体系体现时代性、把握规律性、富于创造性，做到远近结合、上下贯通、内容协调。	To carry out top-level design, it is necessary to have deep insight into the general development trend of the world, accurately grasp the common wishes of the masses, and thoroughly explore the laws of economic and social development, so that the formulated plans and policy systems reflect the times, grasp regularity, and be creative, so as to achieve integration between near and far, vertical integration, and content coordination.	yes
推进中国式现代化是一个探索性事业，还有许多未知领域，需要在实践中去大胆探索，通过改革创新来推动事业发展，决不能刻舟求剑、守株待兔。	Advancing Chinese-style modernization is an exploratory undertaking. There are also many uncharted fields. It requires bold exploration in practice to promote career development through reform and innovation. We must not carve out a sword or wait for the rabbit.	yes
战略问题是一个政党、一个国家的根本性问题。	The strategic issue is a fundamental issue for a political party and a country.	yes
推进中国式现代化，要增强战略的前瞻性，以科学的战略预见未来、引领未来；要增强战略的全局性，着眼于解决事关党和国家事业兴衰成败、牵一发而动全身的重大问题；要增强战略的稳定性，战略一经形成，就要长期坚持、一抓到底、善作善成。	To promote Chinese-style modernization, it is necessary to enhance the forward-looking nature of the strategy, anticipate the future and lead the future with a scientific strategy; it is necessary to enhance the overall nature of the strategy, focus on solving major issues relating to the rise and fall of the cause of the Party and the state and move the whole body; to enhance the stability of the strategy. Once the strategy is formed, it is necessary to persevere for a long time, grasp it to the end, and make good achievements.	yes
要科学把握战略和策略的辩证统一关系，把战略的原则性和策略的灵活性有机结合起来，灵活机动、随机应变、临机决断，在因地制宜、因势而动、顺势而为中把握战略主动。	It is necessary to scientifically grasp the dialectical unification relationship between strategy and strategy, organically combine the principles of strategy with the flexibility of strategy, be flexible, adapt randomly, make ad hoc decisions, and grasp strategic initiative in adapting to local conditions, moving according to the situation, and following the trend.	no
中华民族是守正创新的民族。	The Chinese nation is an honest and innovative nation.	no
处理好守正与创新的关系，既要守好中国式现代化的本和源、根和魂，毫不动摇坚持中国式现代化的中国特色、本质要求、重大原则，确保中国式现代化的正确方向，又要把创新摆在国家发展全局的突出位置，顺应时代发展要求，着眼于解决重大理论和实践问题，积极识变应变求变，大力推进改革创新，不断塑造发展新动能新优势，充分激发全社会创造活力。	To handle the relationship between integrity and innovation, it is necessary not only to protect the origin, roots and soul of Chinese-style modernization, unswervingly adhere to the Chinese characteristics, essential requirements and major principles of Chinese modernization to ensure the correct direction of Chinese-style modernization, but also place innovation in a prominent position in the overall development of the country, conform to the development requirements of the times, focus on solving major theoretical and practical problems, actively recognize change and seek change, and vigorously promote reform and innovation, continuously shape the new advantages of development energy, and fully stimulate the creative vitality of the whole society.	no
效率是公平的重要基础，公平是效率的有力保证。	Efficiency is an important foundation of fairness, and fairness is a strong guarantee of efficiency.	no
我们推进中国式现代化，既要创造比资本主义更高的效率，又要更有效地维护社会公平，更好实现效率与公平相兼顾、相促进、相统一。	To promote Chinese-style modernization, we must not only create higher efficiency than capitalism, but also maintain social fairness more effectively, so as to better balance, promote, and unify efficiency and fairness.	no
处理好效率与公平的关系，不断实现发展为了人民、发展依靠人民、发展成果由人民共享，让现代化建设成果更多更公平惠及全体人民。	Handle the relationship between efficiency and fairness, and continuously achieve development for the people, development depends on the people, and the results of development are shared by the people, so that the achievements of the modernization drive benefit all people more and more fairly.	no
推进中国式现代化，需要处理好活力与秩序的关系，让社会既充满活力又安定有序。	To advance Chinese-style modernization, it is necessary to handle the relationship between vitality and order, so that society is both full of vitality and stability and order.	no
要统筹好发展和安全两件大事，贯彻总体国家安全观，健全国家安全体系，增强维护国家安全能力，坚定维护国家政权安全、制度安全、意识形态安全和重点领域安全。	It is necessary to coordinate the two major issues of development and security, implement the overall national security concept, improve the national security system, enhance the ability to maintain national security, and firmly safeguard the country's regime security, institutional security, ideological security, and security in key areas.	no
既在发展中更多考虑安全因素，通过发展提升国家安全实力，运用发展成果来夯实国家安全的基础，又善于营造有利于经济社会发展的安全环境，不断激发发展活力，实现高质量发展和高水平安全的良性互动。	It not only takes more account of security factors in development, enhances national security strength through development, and uses development achievements to consolidate the foundation of national security, but is also good at creating a safe environment conducive to economic and social development, continuously stimulating development vitality, and achieving healthy interaction between high-quality development and a high level of security.	no
推进中国式现代化，既要坚持走自己的路，又要拓展世界眼光，坚持对外开放，不断拓展中国式现代化的广度和深度。	To promote Chinese-style modernization, we must not only stick to our own path, but also expand our vision of the world, insist on opening up to the outside world, and continuously expand the breadth and depth of Chinese-style modernization.	no
要坚持独立自主、自立自强，坚持把国家和民族发展放在自己力量的基点上，坚持把我国发展进步的命运牢牢掌握在自己手中。	We must insist on independence, self-reliance and self-improvement, insist on placing the development of the country and nation on the basis of our own strength, and insist on firmly grasping the fate of our country's development and progress in our own hands.	no
要不断扩大高水平对外开放，深度参与全球产业分工和合作，用好国内国际两种资源，拓展中国式现代化的发展空间，在互利共赢中共享发展机遇、共创美好未来。	It is necessary to continuously expand a high level of opening-up to the outside world, participate deeply in the division of labor and cooperation in global industries, make good use of both domestic and international resources, expand the development space for Chinese-style modernization, share development opportunities in mutual benefit and win-win situation, and create a better future together.	no
循道而行，方能致远。	You can only get far by following the path.	no
让我们在以习近平同志为核心的党中央坚强领导下、在习近平新时代中国特色社会主义思想科学指引下，把握规律、笃行不怠，充分发挥积极性、主动性、创造性，正确处理好一系列重大关系，在全面建设社会主义现代化国家新征程上奋发有为，不断开辟中国式现代化新境界。	Under the strong leadership of the CPC Central Committee with Comrade Xi Jinping at the core and under the guidance of Xi Jinping's ideology and science of socialism with Chinese characteristics in the new era, let us grasp the rules, give full play to our enthusiasm, initiative, and creativity, properly handle a series of major relationships, work hard on the new journey of comprehensively building a modern socialist country, and continue to open up new horizons of Chinese-style modernization.	no
（德国之声中文网）拜登政府本周五（2月10日）将6个与疑似参与间谍气球计划的中国实体列入黑名单。	(Deutsche Welle Chinese.com) This Friday (February 10), the Biden administration blacklisted 6 Chinese entities suspected of participating in the spy balloon program.	yes
美国商务部表示，这5家中国公司及1家研究机构帮助中国军队现代化，尤其是航空航天项目，包括飞艇和飞机。	The US Department of Commerce said that these 5 Chinese companies and 1 research institute helped modernize the Chinese military, especially aerospace projects, including airships and aircraft.	yes
被列入黑名单的公司很难获得美国的技术出口。	It is difficult for blacklisted companies to obtain US technology exports.	yes
名单被称为“实体名单”（entity list），入列的公司除非获得美国商务部的特别出口许可证，否则将无法向美国供应商购买技术或商品。	The list is called an “entity list” (entity list), and listed companies will not be able to purchase technology or goods from US suppliers unless they obtain a special export license from the US Department of Commerce.	yes
被列入黑名单的公司是：北京南江空天科技股份有限公司、中国电子科技集团第四十八研究所、东莞凌空遥感科技有限公司、鹰门航空科技集团有限公司、广州天海翔航空科技有限公司和山西鹰门航空科技集团有限公司。	The blacklisted companies are: Beijing Nanjiang Aerospace Technology Co., Ltd., 48th Research Institute of China Electronics Technology Group, Dongguan Lingkong Remote Sensing Technology Co., Ltd., Yingmen Aviation Technology Group Co., Ltd., Guangzhou Tianhaixiang Aviation Technology Co., Ltd., and Shanxi Yingmen Aviation Technology Group Co., Ltd.	yes
在此之前，白宫表示考虑做出更广泛措施，“揭露和处理”中国威胁美国国家安全的更大规模监控活动。	Prior to that, the White House said it was considering more extensive measures to “uncover and deal with” China's larger surveillance activities threatening US national security.	yes
气球事件引发中美之间进一步紧张，美国国务卿布林肯取消了访问中国的行程。	The balloon incident triggered further tension between China and the US, and US Secretary of State Brinken cancelled his visit to China.	yes
美国2月4日击落气球，中国政府向美国驻华使馆提出严正交涉，批评美国严重冲击和损害双方稳定中美关系的努力和进程。	The US shot down the balloon on February 4. The Chinese government made serious representations to the US Embassy in China, criticizing the US for seriously impacting and damaging the efforts and progress of the two sides to stabilize Sino-US relations.	yes
从现有残骸证据及中国军方的采购平台资讯，美国政府得出结论，认为该气球的制造厂商“跟中国解放军有直接关系”，而且是中国军方批准的供应商。	From existing evidence of the wreckage and information from the Chinese military's procurement platform, the US government has concluded that the manufacturer of the balloon “has a direct relationship with the Chinese People's Liberation Army” and that it is a supplier approved by the Chinese military.	yes
中国外交部发言人毛宁在周五的新闻发布会上表示，关于一只中国无人民用飞艇因不可抗力误入美国领空的意外事件，中方已经多次说明情况、阐明立场。	Chinese Foreign Ministry spokesman Mao Ning said at a press conference on Friday that China has explained the situation and clarified its position on the accident where a Chinese airship with no people mistakenly entered US airspace due to force majeure.	yes
根据外交部网站，她补充表示，美国国会的有关决议案纯属政治操弄和炒作。	According to the Ministry of Foreign Affairs website, she added that the relevant US congressional resolution was pure political manipulation and hype.	no
中方对此强烈不满、坚决反对。	The Chinese side is strongly dissatisfied and resolutely opposed to this.	no
美国商务部负责出口执法的助理部长阿克塞尔罗德(Matthew Axelrod)表示： “今天的行动表明，我们查明并阻止中国使用间谍气球而做出的共同努力，这些气球侵犯了美国和40多个国家的领空。	Matthew Axelrod (Matthew Axelrod), Assistant Secretary of Commerce in charge of export enforcement at the US Department of Commerce, said: “Today's action shows that we have identified and stopped China's joint efforts to use spy balloons. （德国之声中文网）距离土耳其和叙利亚部分地区发生地震已经过去数日，找到幸存者的希望日渐渺茫，然而在周六获救的一家五口却令搜救人员感到无比欣慰。	(Deutsche Welle Chinese.com) A few days have passed since the earthquakes occurred in Turkey and parts of Syria, and hopes of finding survivors are getting slimmer. However, a family of five rescued on Saturday made search and rescue personnel extremely happy.	yes
据美联社报道，在加济安泰普省的重灾区努尔达伊镇，这个五口之家在废墟之下受困五天多之后，被成功营救。	According to the Associated Press, in the hardest-hit town of Nurdai in Gaziantep province, this family of five was successfully rescued after being stranded under ruins for more than five days.	yes
搜救人员先是从一堆废墟中拉出了母亲和女儿，随后找到了父亲，但他坚持要求先救自己的儿子和另一个女儿。	Search and rescue personnel first pulled the mother and daughter out of the rubble, then found the father, but he insisted that his son and another daughter be saved first.	yes
当他们全部获救之后，人群中响起了欢呼声。	When they had all been rescued, there was cheering in the crowd.	yes
在土耳其南部城市卡赫拉曼马拉什，在恶劣的严寒天气条件下，一个16岁的少年和一位70岁老妪也被成功营救。	In the southern Turkish city of Kahramanmaras, under severe cold weather conditions, a 16-year-old teenager and a 70-year-old elder were also successfully rescued.	yes

目前根据官方统计，周一的地震已经在土耳其造成超过2万人死亡，邻国叙利亚的死亡人数估计在3500人以上。	Currently, according to official statistics, the earthquake on Monday has killed more than 20,000 people in Turkey, and the death toll in neighboring Syria is estimated to be over 3,500.	yes
尽管专家表示，人在被困废墟之后最多还能存活一周以上的时间，但是寻找到更多幸存者的希望已经变得愈加渺茫。	Although experts say people can survive for at most a week or more after being trapped in ruins, hopes of finding more survivors have become increasingly slim.	no
救援人员仍然在借助热成像仪来探寻废墟之下的生命迹象。	Rescuers are still using thermal imagers to search for signs of life under the rubble.	no
与此同时，救援工作的重点开始转向帮助那些急需救助的幸存者。	Meanwhile, the focus of rescue efforts began to shift to helping survivors in desperate need of help.	no
联合国官员：该地区“百年未遇”的灾难	UN official: A disaster the region has “not seen in 100 years”	no
主管人道主义事务的联合国副秘书长兼紧急救济协调员马丁·格里菲思（Martin Griffiths）在土耳其召开的记者会上表示，这次地震是该地区“百年以来最糟糕的一次灾难”。	UN Under-Secretary-General for Humanitarian Affairs and Emergency Relief Coordinator Martin Griffiths (Martin Griffiths) said at a press conference in Turkey that the earthquake was “the worst disaster in 100 years” in the region.	no
他还称赞土耳其在灾后的应对行动是“非同寻常”的。	He also praised Turkey's response in the aftermath of the disaster as “extraordinary.”	no

60年来全球发生的破坏性最强的大地震	The most devastating earthquake in the world in 60 years	no
智利大地震（1960年）	The Great Chilean Earthquake (1960)	no
当地时间1960年5月22日下午3点11分，智利瓦尔迪维亚发生人类史上观测记录到的规模最大的地震，地震矩规模为9.5。	At 3:11 p.m. local time on May 22, 1960, the largest earthquake ever observed and recorded in human history occurred in Valdivia, Chile. The magnitude of the earthquake was 9.5.	no
短短十分钟内，瓦尔迪维亚整座城市变为废墟。	Within ten minutes, the entire city of Valdivia was in ruins.	no
地震之后引发的巨大海啸袭击到智利海岸线，掀起浪高高度是25米高的巨大海啸。	The massive tsunami triggered after the earthquake hit the Chilean coastline, setting off a massive tsunami with waves 25 meters high.	no
海啸波及到遥远的日本、菲律宾。	The tsunami affected as far away as Japan and the Philippines.	no
如此范围的灾难所造成的罹难人数以及经济损失无法精确得知。	The number of victims and economic losses caused by disasters of this magnitude cannot be accurately known.	no
60年来全球发生的破坏性最强的大地震	The most devastating earthquake in the world in 60 years	no
阿拉斯加大地震（1964年）	Alaska earthquake (1964)	no
1964年3月27日是一个星期五，也是是耶稣受难日。	March 27, 1964 is a Friday, and it's also Good Friday.	no
这一天美国阿拉斯加发生北美洲历史上最大的地震，矩震级达到9.2。	On this day, the largest earthquake in North American history occurred in Alaska, USA. The magnitude of the earthquake reached 9.2.	no
直到2006年，阿拉斯加大地震仍然是有纪录以来世界第三大地震。	Until 2006, the Alaska earthquake was still the third largest earthquake in the world on record.	no
地震发生时，太平洋板块和北美洲板块之间的一个断层在威廉王子湾接近学院峡湾的地方断裂。	At the time of the earthquake, a fault between the Pacific plate and the North American plate broke in Prince William Bay near College Fjord.	no
在大部分的地区这场地震持续了3分钟到5分钟。	The earthquake lasted 3 to 5 minutes in most regions.	no
海床位移引发了巨大的海啸，高度为67米。	Seabed displacement triggered a massive tsunami at a height of 67 meters.	no
由于当天是假日，所以学校和许多企业都关闭了。	Since that day was a holiday, schools and many businesses were closed.	no
这场大地震最后导致了139人罹难。	In the end, 139 people died as a result of this massive earthquake.	no
其中9人直接死于地震，其他130人死于地震引发的海啸。	Of these, 9 people died directly from the earthquake, while 130 others died from the tsunami caused by the earthquake.	no
60年来全球发生的破坏性最强的大地震	The most devastating earthquake in the world in 60 years	no
唐山大地震（1976年）	The Great Tangshan Earthquake (1976)	no
1976年7月28日，中国河北省唐山市和丰南县在16小时内发生两次7级以上强烈地震。	On July 28, 1976, two strong earthquakes of magnitude 7 or above occurred within 16 hours in Tangshan City and Fengnan County in Hebei Province, China.	no
震源距地面23千米。	The epicenter was 23 km from the ground.	no
唐山市全市交通、通讯、供水、供电中断，顷刻间被夷为平地。	The entire city of Tangshan City's traffic, communications, water supply, and electricity supply was interrupted, and it was instantly razed to the ground.	no
140公里外的首都北京也有强烈震感。	A strong shock was also felt in the capital Beijing, 140 kilometers away.	no
据官方统计，包括北京、天津在内的所有受灾地区，地震造成242769人死亡，164851人重伤。	According to official statistics, the earthquake killed 242,769 people and seriously injured 16,4851 in all affected areas, including Beijing and Tianjin.	no
唐山大地震成为中国有记录至今第二多人死亡的地震，仅次于1556年嘉靖大地震。	The Tangshan earthquake became the second most fatal earthquake ever recorded in China, after the 1556 Jiajing earthquake.	no
但是有海外科学家估计，这场地震可能造成至少65万人死亡。	However, some overseas scientists estimate that at least 650,000 people may have died as a result of the earthquake.	no
60年来全球发生的破坏性最强的大地震	The most devastating earthquake in the world in 60 years	no
印度洋大地震（2004年）	The Great Indian Ocean Earthquake (2004)	no
2004年12月26日，印尼苏门答腊岛亚齐省西岸160公里处发生地震，震源深度30公里，矩震级9.1到9.3。	On December 26, 2004, an earthquake occurred 160 kilometers west of Aceh province in Sumatra, Indonesia. The depth of the earthquake was 30 kilometers, and the magnitude of the earthquake was 9.1 to 9.3.	no
地震引发了浪高高度达15到30米的巨大海啸。	The earthquake triggered a massive tsunami with waves 15 to 30 meters high.	no
太平洋沿岸总共14个国家被波及，其中受灾严重最严重的地区包括印尼亚齐省、泰国镐立和普吉岛渡假区、斯里兰卡和印度泰米尔邦。	A total of 14 countries along the Pacific coast were affected, including Indonesia's Qi province, Gauri and Phuket resorts in Thailand, Sri Lanka, and the Indian state of Tamil.	no
当时正值圣诞节的旅游旺季，受灾地区聚集了大量的旅客和本地居民，导致许多在沙滩上享受假期的旅客和在海边工作的当地人被海啸卷到海底，使这次地震不少人成为失踪者。	It was the peak Christmas tourist season at the time, and a large number of tourists and local residents gathered in the affected area. As a result, many travelers enjoying their holidays on the beach and locals working at the seaside were swept to the bottom of the sea by the tsunami, causing many people to disappear from this earthquake.	no
据估计，罹难人数和失踪人数至少有30万人。	It is estimated that at least 300,000 people have died and disappeared.	no

是中华人民共和国成立以来破坏力最大的地震，也是唐山大地震后伤亡最惨重的一次。	It was the most destructive earthquake since the founding of the People's Republic of China and the worst casualties since the Tangshan earthquake.	no

日本东北大地震（2011年）	The Great Tohoku Earthquake in Japan (2011)	no
2011年3月11日日本东北地方外海发生矩震级为9.0的大型逆冲区地震。	On 2011/3/11, a large-scale reverse earthquake with a magnitude of 9.0 occurred off the coast of the Tohoku region of Japan.	no
震中位于在宫城县首府仙台市以东的太平洋海域，震源深度测得数据为24千米，并且引发最大爬高40.1米的巨大海啸。	The epicenter was located in the Pacific Ocean east of Sendai City, the capital of Miyagi Prefecture. The depth of the earthquake was measured at 24 kilometers, and it triggered a massive tsunami with a maximum elevation of 40.1 meters.	no
这场地震是日本有观测纪录到以来第一个震级超过9的地震。	This earthquake was the first earthquake with a magnitude greater than 9 since Japan had observational records.	no
约有2.2万人在灾害丧生，大约40万座建筑被完全摧毁或倒塌。	About 22,000 people died in the disaster, and about 400,000 buildings were completely destroyed or collapsed.	no

防骗提示：	Anti-scam tips:	yes
1. 多关注网络安全资讯，提高个人防范意识；	1. Pay more attention to cybersecurity information to raise personal awareness of prevention;	yes
2. 切勿随便登入来历不明的网站并在网站内登记个人及信用卡资料，以防遭人盗用；	2. Do not casually log in to websites of unknown origin and register personal and credit card information on the website to prevent misappropriation;	yes
3. 警惕假冒网站及钓鱼网站，时刻留意网站网址是否与官方网站完全相符；	3. Be wary of fake websites and phishing websites, and always check whether the website URL completely matches the official website;	yes
4. 为手机、移动装置或电脑安装防毒软件，并定期更新；	4. Install anti-virus software for your phone, mobile device, or computer, and update it regularly;	yes

他表示，要深入学习贯彻习近平总书记在研讨班开班式上的重要讲话精神，更加坚定拥护“两个确立”、坚决做到“两个维护”，增强本领、真抓实干，扎实推进中国式现代化各项工作，在全面建设社会主义现代化国家、全面推进中华民族伟大复兴中创造经得起历史、实践和人民检验的业绩。	He said that it is necessary to thoroughly study and implement the spirit of General Secretary Xi Jinping's important speech at the opening ceremony of the seminar, more firmly support the “two establishments”, resolutely carry out the “two maintenance”, strengthen our abilities, really work hard, solidly push forward all aspects of Chinese-style modernization, and create achievements that can stand the test of history, practice and people in comprehensively advancing the great rejuvenation of the Chinese nation.	yes
研讨班期间，全体学员以习近平新时代中国特色社会主义思想为指导，认真学习党的二十大精神和习近平总书记在研讨班开班式上的重要讲话，联系实际深入研讨交流，深化了对中国式现代化一系列重大理论和实践问题的认识，增强了在以习近平同志为核心的党中央坚强领导下以中国式现代化全面推进中华民族伟大复兴的信心和决心，增强了履职尽责、做好工作、确保新时代新征程良好开局的责任感和使命感。	During the seminar, all participants were guided by Xi Jinping's ideology of socialism with Chinese characteristics in the new era, carefully studied the spirit of the 20th National Congress of the Party and General Secretary Xi Jinping's important speech at the opening ceremony of the seminar, deepened their understanding of a series of major theoretical and practical issues of Chinese-style modernization, strengthened their confidence and determination to comprehensively advance the great rejuvenation of the Chinese nation with Chinese modernization under the strong leadership of the CPC Central Committee with Comrade Xi Jinping at the core, enhanced their sense of responsibility and mission to perform their duties with due diligence, work well, and ensure a good start to the new journey in the new era.	yes
结业式上，研讨班10名代表发言，汇报交流了学习收获。	At the graduation ceremony, 10 seminar delegates spoke and shared their learning gains.	yes
蔡奇表示，学习贯彻习近平新时代中国特色社会主义思想和党的二十大精神，既是当前和今后一个时期的首要政治任务，也是一项长期战略任务，要按照“全面学习、全面把握、全面落实”的要求，推动学习贯彻工作不断往深里走、往实里走、往心里走。	Cai Qi said that studying and implementing Xi Jinping's ideology of socialism with Chinese characteristics in the new era and the spirit of the 20th National Congress of the Party is not only a top political task at present and in the coming period, but also a long-term strategic task. In accordance with the requirements of “comprehensive study, comprehensive grasp, and comprehensive implementation,” it is necessary to push the study and implementation work to continue to go deep, factual, and to the heart.	yes
要更加深刻领悟“两个确立”的决定性意义，坚决维护习近平总书记的核心地位、维护党中央权威和集中统一领导，不断提高政治判断力、政治领悟力、政治执行力，始终在思想上政治上行动上同以习近平同志为核心的党中央保持高度一致。	We must have a deeper understanding of the decisive significance of the “two establishment”, resolutely uphold the central position of General Secretary Xi Jinping, maintain the authority of the Party Central Committee and centralize unified leadership, continuously improve our political judgment, political understanding, and political execution, and always maintain a high degree of consistency with the Party Central Committee with Comrade Xi Jinping at the core in ideological and political actions.	yes
要努力掌握好马克思主义理论这一看家本领，自觉用党的创新理论武装头脑、指导实践、推动工作，在深学、细悟、笃行上下功夫，真正学出坚定信念、学出绝对忠诚、学出使命担当。	We must work hard to master Marxist theory, which is the masterful ability of Marxist theory, consciously arm our minds with the Party's innovative theories, guide practice, and promote work, and work hard in depth study, careful study, and practice, and truly learn firm beliefs, learn absolute loyalty, and learn responsibility for our mission.	yes
要以奋发有为的精神状态贯彻落实好党的二十大各项决策部署，扎实推进中国式现代化，撸起袖子加油干，扑下身子当好“施工队长”，一步一个脚印把蓝图变为现实。	We must work hard to implement the decisions and arrangements of the 20th National Congress of the Party, solidly push forward Chinese-style modernization, roll up our sleeves and work hard, throw down our bodies and be a good “construction captain,” and turn the blueprint into reality step by step.	no

要增强推动高质量发展本领、服务群众本领、防范化解风险本领，大兴调查研究之风，坚决防止和克服形式主义、官僚主义。	It is necessary to strengthen the ability to promote high-quality development, serve the masses, prevent and mitigate risks, promote the style of investigation and research, and resolutely prevent and overcome formalism and bureaucracy.	no

Google AI聊天机器人“答错问题” 母公司股价蒸发千亿美元	The stock price of the parent company of Google's AI chatbot “answered the wrong question” evaporated by 100 billion US dollars	yes
（综合11日电）	(Comprehensive report from the 11th)	yes
Google新推出的人工智能聊天机器人Bard出师不利，在宣传短片中“答错问题”，导致Google母公司Alphabet股价周三一度急挫8.9%，跌破100美元大关，市值蒸发1100亿美元（约4765亿令吉），截至周五闭市报94.57美元。	Google's newly launched artificial intelligence chatbot, Bard, was at a disadvantage. It “answered the wrong question” in the promotional video, causing the stock price of Google's parent company Alphabet to plummet 8.9% on Wednesday, falling below the $100 mark, and the market capitalization evaporated by 110 billion US dollars (about RM476.5 billion). As of Friday's market closing report was 94.57 US dollars.	yes
市场担心Alphabet不及竞争对手微软。	The market is worried that Alphabet will fall short of rival Microsoft.	yes
根据《路透社》报道，google较早时在社交媒体发布AI聊天机器人Bard的宣传短片，片中有人询问Bard：“我可以告诉我9岁的孩子关于James Webb太空望远镜 (JWST) 的哪些新发现？	According to the “Reuters” report, Google posted a promotional video for the AI chatbot Bard on social media earlier. In the video, someone asked Bard: “Can I tell my 9-year-old child what new discoveries about the James Webb Space Telescope (JWST) have been discovered?	yes
”Bard在回答中提到该望远镜曾拍摄到太阳系外行星的第一张照片。	” In response, Bard mentioned that the telescope had taken the first picture of a planet outside our solar system.	yes
不过，根据美国国家航空航天局资料，太阳系外行星的第一张照片是由欧洲南方天文台的“甚大望远镜”于2004年所拍。	However, according to NASA data, the first picture of a planet outside the solar system was taken by the European Southern Observatory's “Very Large Telescope” in 2004.	yes
《路透社》更以“Bard回答错误后Alphabet股价暴跌”为题报道。	“Reuters” also reported on the title “Alphabet's stock price plummeted after Bard gave a wrong answer.”	yes
另一方面，Google指出，Bard的回应“突显了严格测试过程的重要性”，会把外部反馈与自己的内部测试结合起来，以确保Bard的回应“在质量、安全和真实信息的基础上达到高标准”。	On the other hand, Google notes that Bard's response “highlights the importance of a rigorous testing process” and will combine external feedback with his own internal testing to ensure that Bard's response “meets high standards based on quality, security, and real information.”	yes
新加坡旅游业复苏强劲 入境旅客比2021年增长19倍	Singapore's tourism industry is recovering strongly, and the number of inbound visitors increased 19 times over 2021	yes
（综合11日电）新加坡旅游局近日公布，预计2023年到访新加坡的国际旅客人次可达1200万至1400万，将带来约180亿至210亿新元的旅游收益；旅客人次和旅游收入将恢复到2019年新冠疫情前约67%至75%的水平；2024年旅游业实现全面复苏的可能性很大。	(Comprehensive report of the 11th) The Singapore Tourism Board recently announced that it expects the number of international visitors to Singapore to reach 12 million to 14 million in 2023, bringing in about 18 billion to 21 billion Singapore dollars in tourism revenue; the number of visitors and tourism revenue will return to the level of about 67% to 75% before the COVID-19 pandemic in 2019; and there is a high possibility that the tourism industry will fully recover in 2024.	yes
2022年新加坡旅游市场逐步重新启动和恢复。	The Singapore travel market will gradually restart and recover in 2022.	yes
新加坡旅游局最新发布的统计数据显示，2022年入境旅客从2021年的33.06万人次增长19倍，达到630万人次，超越旅游局早前预估的400万至600万人次，游客已经恢复至疫情前33%的水平。	According to the latest statistics released by the Singapore Tourism Board, the number of inbound visitors in 2022 increased 19 times from 330,600 in 2021 to 6.3 million, surpassing the MGTO's earlier estimate of 4 million to 6 million, and visitors have recovered to the level of 33% before the pandemic.	yes
2022年1月至9月，新加坡旅游收入共计89.6亿新元，预计2022年全年旅游收入可达138亿至143亿新元，比2021年的18.9亿新元增长6倍至7倍，已经恢复到2019年新冠疫情前约50%至52%的水平。	From January to September 2022, Singapore's tourism revenue totaled S$8.96 billion. It is estimated that tourism revenue for the full year of 2022 will reach S$13.8 billion to S$14.3 billion, an increase of 6 to 7 times over S$1.89 billion in 2021. It has returned to the level of about 50% to 52% before the COVID-19 pandemic in 2019.	yes
新加坡政府多措并举，加速旅游业复苏。	The Singapore government has taken a number of measures to accelerate the recovery of the tourism industry.	yes
2022年4月，政府宣布拨款近5亿新元用来刺激旅游业复苏。	In April 2022, the government announced an allocation of nearly S$500 million to stimulate the recovery of the tourism industry.	yes
旅游局日前宣布，将计划在未来两年从这笔预算中拨出1.1亿新元，推出更多商业和休闲活动吸引旅客回流。	The MGTO announced a few days ago that it plans to allocate S$110 million from this budget over the next two years to launch more commercial and leisure activities to attract travelers back.	yes
为了使健康养生成为新加坡的旅游亮点之一，新加坡旅游局在2022年11月23日发布了一份意向征集活动，计划在新加坡南部海岸开发一个健康养生景点。	In order to make health and wellness one of Singapore's tourist highlights, the Singapore Tourism Board announced a call for intentions on November 23, 2022, planning to develop a health and wellness attraction on the southern coast of Singapore.	yes
新加坡旅游局体育与康养旅游执行署长王凌丽说，近年来，越来越多的游客把身体健康放在各项考虑因素的首位。	Wang Lingli, Executive Director of Sports and Wellness Tourism of the Singapore Tourism Board, said that in recent years, more and more tourists have placed physical health at the top of all considerations.	yes
在拥有滨海湾花园、滨海堤坝的滨海南区开发一个健康养生景点，有望为新加坡的旅游业和经济作出贡献，让游客在新加坡消费并逗留更久。	The development of a health and wellness attraction in the Binhai South Area, which has Gardens by the Bay and the Waterfront Embankment, is expected to contribute to Singapore's tourism and economy, allowing visitors to spend and stay in Singapore longer.	no
新加坡旅游局局长陈建隆表示，未来几年内，健康养生将成为新加坡旅游产品的重要组成部分。	Singapore Tourism Board Director Chan Kin-lung said that in the next few years, health and wellness will become an important part of Singapore's tourism products.	no
新冠疫情提升了公众对于身体和心理健康的认知和需求。	The COVID-19 pandemic has increased public awareness and demand for physical and mental health.	no
为此，过去两年旅游局一直向本地公众和国际游客推广健康养生项目。	To this end, the Tourism Board has been promoting health and wellness programs to the local public and international tourists for the past two years.	no
2022年6月，新加坡旅游局举办了首届健康养生节，为公众提供了130多项各类健康活动和体验。	In June 2022, the Singapore Tourism Board hosted the first Health and Wellness Festival, providing the public with more than 130 health activities and experiences of all kinds.	no
新加坡将持续为游客提供新的旅行体验。	Singapore will continue to provide visitors with new travel experiences.	no
除新开放的新加坡儿童博物馆、滨海湾花园的阿凡达世界、圣淘沙中央海滩市集、艺术科学博物馆新增的“探索新领域”展厅，以及夜间野生动物园新建的露天剧场外，旅游局将支持万态野生动物世界的飞禽公园等项目发展与更新，使新加坡成为具有吸引力的国际旅行地。	In addition to the newly opened Singapore Children's Museum, Avatar World at Gardens by the Bay, Sentosa Central Beach Market, the Sentosa Central Beach Market, and the new “Exploring New Frontiers” exhibition hall at the Art and Science Museum, the MGTO will support the development and renewal of projects such as Wantai Wildlife World's Bird Park, making Singapore an attractive international travel destination.	no
按照计划，新加坡将于2023年年内制定会议、会展与奖励旅游业可持续发展的相关行业标准，并着重改善废物处理和碳排放两大方面的问题，进一步优化旅游环境。	According to the plan, Singapore will set relevant industry standards for conferences, exhibitions and incentives for the sustainable development of the tourism industry within 2023, and focus on improving the two major issues of waste treatment and carbon emissions to further optimize the tourism environment.	no
新加坡旅游业的复苏加快了航空业复苏。	The recovery of Singapore's tourism industry has accelerated the recovery of the aviation industry.	no
数据显示，截至2022年12月18日，樟宜机场客流量强劲复苏，每天接待的乘客已多达15万人次，每周约100万人次，相当于新冠疫情前的75%左右，航空业员工在岗数量也已经恢复到疫情前约90%的水平。	According to the data, as of December 18, 2022, passenger traffic at Changi Airport has recovered strongly. It has received 150,000 passengers every day, about 1 million passengers per week, which is equivalent to about 75% of what it was before the COVID-19 pandemic. The number of employees working in the aviation industry has also returned to about 90% of the pre-pandemic level.	no
数据显示，2022年1月至10月新加坡已接待旅客2360万人次，相当于新冠疫情前的42%，起降航班17万架次，是疫情前的53%。	According to the data, from January to October 2022, Singapore has received 23.6 million visitors, equivalent to 42% before the COVID-19 pandemic. The number of flights taking off and landing was 170,000, which is 53% of what it was before the pandemic.	no
旅游业快速复苏，也带动了住宿、交通、餐饮和购物等行业的复苏步伐。	The rapid recovery of the tourism industry has also driven the pace of recovery in industries such as accommodation, transportation, catering and shopping.	no
新加坡政府和旅游业对中国市场寄予厚望。	The Singapore government and the tourism industry have high hopes for the Chinese market.	no
新加坡旅游局国际司助理局长柯淑丹说，中国旅行平台的一项调查显示，新加坡的安全指数位列全球前三，这也是新加坡深受中国游客喜爱的原因之一。	Ke Shudan, Assistant Director of the International Department of the Singapore Tourism Board, said that according to a survey by a Chinese travel platform, Singapore's safety index ranks in the top three in the world. This is also one of the reasons why Singapore is loved by Chinese tourists.	no
新冠疫情前，中国每年有约360万人次到新加坡旅行度假。	Before the COVID-19 pandemic, China traveled to Singapore every year for about 3.6 million vacations.	no
随着中国放宽边境政策，预计今年中国游客人次可恢复至2019年的三成至六成。	As China relaxes its border policy, the number of Chinese tourists is expected to return to 30% to 60% of 2019 this year.	no
柯淑丹指出，接下来，旅游局将密切关注中国针对出境旅行政策进一步释放的信号，以应对游客需求的变化。	Ko Shudan pointed out that next, the MGTO will pay close attention to further signals released by China regarding outbound travel policies to cope with changes in tourist demand.	no
新加坡旅游局除与携程等中国线上旅行平台、旅行社强化伙伴关系外，将针对中国境外游出现的新趋势，积极做好接待中国游客的准备。	In addition to strengthening partnerships with Chinese online travel platforms and travel agencies such as Ctrip, the Singapore Tourism Board will actively prepare to welcome Chinese tourists in response to the new trends emerging in travel outside of China.	no
展望2023年旅游市场，新加坡旅游局充满信心，认为全球经济只要不出现显著衰退影响公众收入，以及不再有新的大面积致命疫情暴发等情况出现，旅游业复苏步伐将快于预期。	Looking ahead to the 2023 travel market, the Singapore Tourism Board is confident that as long as there is no significant recession in the global economy affecting public revenue and there are no new large-scale fatal outbreaks, the pace of tourism recovery will be faster than expected.	no
金正恩父女互动亲密 老婆遭冷落一旁	Kim Jong-un's father and daughter interacted with his close wife were snubbed	yes
（综合11日电）朝鲜8日晚间举行建军节第75周年阅兵仪式，领导人金正恩的女儿金主爱不仅出席，还与父亲一同站上主席台。	(General report of 11th) On the evening of the 8th, North Korea held a military parade for the 75th anniversary of Army Day. Kim Ju-ae, the daughter of leader Kim Jong-un, not only attended, but also stood on the podium with her father.	yes
朝鲜官媒9日公布影片，金主爱依偎在父亲身边，数次温情对视、讲悄悄话，她用双手轻捧老爸的脸颊，甚至摸著父亲胸口，父女互动画面播送至举国上下。	North Korea's official media released a video on the 9th. Kim Ju-ae snuggled up to her father, looked at her father warmly and whispered several times. She patted her father's cheek with her hands and even touched her father's chest. The interactive footage of the father and daughter was broadcast all over the country.	yes
然而，第一夫人李雪主只能退到一旁。	However, the first lady Li Xuezhu was only able to back off.	yes
综合韩国“朝鲜新闻”等报导，金正恩、李雪主夫妇7日带著女儿金主爱出席晚宴的官方合照中，金主爱不仅罕见坐在父母正中间C位，在隔日晚间建军节第75周年阅兵仪式上，她还与金正恩一起登上主席台。	According to reports from South Korea's “North Korea News” and other reports, in the official group photo of Kim Jong-un and Lee Seok-joo attending the dinner on the 7th with their daughter Kim Joo Ae, Kim Joo Ae not only rarely sits in C position in the middle of her parents; at the military parade on the 75th anniversary of Army Day the next night, she also appeared on the podium with Kim Jong-un.	yes
朝鲜官媒“朝鲜中央电视台”事后释出阅兵式影片，曝光了更多父女情深的画面。	The North Korean official media “North Korea Central Television” later released a military parade video, which revealed more images of the father and daughter being affectionate.	yes
金正恩在主席台上数次与女儿对望，两人脸上的笑容从未退去，还互相在耳边讲悄悄话，金主爱一度以双手捧起老爸的两颊，金正恩也以灿笑回应。	Kim Jong-un confronted her daughter several times on the podium. The smiles on their faces never went back. They also kept quiet messages in each other's ears. At one point, Kim Joo-ae picked up her dad's cheeks with both hands, and Kim Jong-un also responded with a big smile.	yes
其他官媒画面也显示，金主爱与金正恩坐在室内沙发椅上时，用手不断摸著父亲的脸；她与父亲挽著手走路时，一边用手摸在金正恩的胸口。	Other official media footage also showed that when Kim Joo Ae and Kim Jong-un were sitting on an indoor sofa chair, they constantly touched her father's face with her hands; while she walked hand in hand with her father, she touched Kim Jong-un's chest with her hands.	yes
而第一夫人李雪主全程只能走在后头或是坐在一旁，总是距离丈夫和女儿有几步之差。	However, the first lady, Li Xuezhu, can only walk or sit on the side the whole time; she is always a few steps away from her husband and daughter.	yes

重阳问答︱如何看待美国1月非农就业数据大超预期及未来趋势 - 经济观察网 － 专业财经新闻网站	Chongyang Q&A | How do you view the US non-farm payrolls data for January exceeding expectations and future trends - Economic Watch － A professional financial news website	yes
Q：请问重阳投资，如何看待美国1月非农就业数据大超预期及未来趋势？	Q: May I ask Chongyang Investment, what do you think of the US non-farm payrolls data for January exceeding expectations and future trends?	yes
A：2月3日美国劳工部公布2023年1月非农就业数据，新增非农就业51.7万人，大幅高于市场预期的18.9万人；失业率降至3.4%，为近50年以来的最低位；时薪同比增速4.4%，环比增速0.3%，略有放缓。	A: On February 3, the US Department of Labor released non-farm payrolls data for January 2023, adding 517,000 new non-farm payrolls, significantly higher than market expectations of 189,000; the unemployment rate fell to 3.4%, the lowest level in nearly 50 years; hourly wages grew 4.4% year on year and 0.3% month on month, a slight slowdown.	yes
从总量上来看，本次数据存在很多一次性和技术性因素的扰动，比如罢工返岗的教职工、调查统计口径的修正、季调因子的更新，后续可能将有所修正（参考2022年1月新增非农由50.4万人下修至36.4万人），非农就业或不像数据体现的那样强劲。	In terms of total volume, there are many one-time and technical disturbances in this data, such as faculty and staff on strike and returning to work, revisions to survey statistics, and updates to seasonal factors. There may be future revisions (see the addition of 504,000 non-farmers in January 2022, downgraded from 504,000 to 364,000 people). Non-farm payrolls may not be as strong as reflected in the data.	yes
从结构上来看，高科技企业裁员影响仍在，但占比较低；高接触性服务业如休闲酒店、教育保健等新增就业大幅回升，数据显示服务业劳动力缺口仍存。	From a structural point of view, the impact of layoffs in high-tech enterprises is still there, but the share is relatively low; new jobs in high-contact service industries such as leisure hotels, education and health care have rebounded sharply, and data shows that there is still a labor gap in the service industry.	yes
结合同样大超预期的服务业PMI、岗位空缺和劳动力缺口数据的回升和消费信贷数据的强势，我们判断经过极端天气和节假日后美国服务业迎来了快速修复。	Combined with the service sector PMI that far exceeded expectations, the recovery in job vacancies and labor gap data, and the strength of consumer credit data, we judge that the US service sector ushered in a rapid recovery after extreme weather and holidays.	yes
我们认为，在不经过衰退的情况下美国就业市场的供需紧张难以改善。	We believe that it is difficult to improve tight supply and demand in the US job market without going through a recession.	yes
目前美国劳动力市场尚有500余万的供给缺口，而劳动参与率上行缓慢，尤其是25-54岁劳动参与率已经接近疫情前高点。	Currently, there is still a supply gap of more than 5 million in the US labor market, and the labor participation rate is rising slowly. In particular, the labor participation rate of 25-54 year olds is already close to the high before the epidemic.	yes
除此之外，由于美国居民超额储蓄和消费信贷的强势，消费需求的强劲将促使紧缩政策对就业市场的影响进一步滞后。	In addition to this, strong consumer demand will further delay the impact of austerity policies on the job market due to excess savings of American residents and strong consumer credit.	yes

随着通胀数据的持续改善，美联储在缩短加息步伐的同时还不断维系着市场通胀预期脆弱的平衡，但市场对于美联储偏向鹰派的表述视而不见，不仅预期提前停止加息，还预期年末两次降息。	As inflation data continues to improve, while shortening the pace of interest rate hikes, the Fed continues to maintain the weak balance of market inflation expectations. However, the market has turned a blind eye to the Fed's hawkish statement. It not only expects an early cessation of interest rate hikes, but also expects two interest rate cuts at the end of the year.	no
在劳动力市场供需紧张，紧缩政策影响不明的情况下，我们认为美联储年末对于加息的指引是相对合理的，市场极端预期的调整和交易的拥挤或将对市场产生一定伤害。	In a situation where supply and demand in the labor market are tight and the impact of austerity policies is unclear, we believe that the Fed's guidance on raising interest rates at the end of the year is relatively reasonable, and that adjustments to extreme market expectations and the congestion of transactions may cause some damage to the market.	no
尽管如此，薪资增速的顽固难改当前通胀快速下降的趋势，随着M2数据同比转负以及各个CPI分项领先指标的逐渐转好，自10月份以来美国CPI数据已经转向快速下降阶段，薪资增速的顽固仅会对以后的通胀数据形成托底，当前的市场预期难以证伪，在下一期通胀数据公布后市场或进入新一轮博弈。	Despite this, the stubbornness of the wage growth rate is difficult to reverse the current trend of rapid decline in inflation. 杉杉创始人郑永刚因突发心脏疾病过世 曾带领中国服装第一股转型 - 经济观察网 － 专业财经新闻网站	Zheng Yonggang, founder of Shanshan, passed away due to a sudden heart disease and led the transformation of the first line of clothing in China - Economic Watch － A professional financial news website	yes
经济观察网 记者 郑淯心 2月11日，认证主体为杉杉控股有限公司（以下简称“杉杉控股 ” ） 的微信公众号发布讣告，杉杉企业创始人、杉杉控股董事局主席郑永刚因突发心脏疾病救治无效，于2023年2月10日去世，享年65岁。	On February 11, Zheng Jixin, a reporter from the Economic Watch Network, published an obituary on the WeChat account of Shanshan Holdings Co., Ltd. (hereinafter referred to as “Shanshan Holdings”). Zheng Yonggang, founder of Shanshan Enterprise and chairman of the board of directors of Shanshan Holdings, died on February 10, 2023 at the age of 65 due to ineffective treatment for a sudden heart disease.	yes
上世纪80年代，郑永刚担任国营棉纺厂的厂长，随着调任，1989年郑永刚成为杉杉股份的前身宁波云港服装总厂的厂长。	In the 80s of the last century, Zheng Yonggang was the factory manager of a state-owned cotton spinning factory. Following his transfer, Zheng Yonggang became the factory manager of Ningbo Yungang Garment Factory, the predecessor of Shanshan Co., Ltd. in 1989.	yes
2022年12月，在第二十届中国企业领袖年会暨第二十二届中国企业未来之星年会上，郑永刚在演讲中称，在上世纪90年代的中国西服市场，杉杉品牌的市占率曾高达37 % 。	In December 2022, at the 20th Annual Conference of Chinese Business Leaders and the 22nd Annual Conference of Chinese Business Future Stars, Zheng Yonggang said in his speech that in the Chinese suit market in the 90s of the last century, the market share of the Shanshan brand was as high as 37 percent.	yes
1996年杉杉股份（600884.SH）上市，成为中国服装业第一家上市公司。	In 1996, Shanshan Co., Ltd. (600884.SH) went public, becoming the first listed company in the Chinese garment industry.	yes
就在服装业务如日中天时，杉杉集团却开始转型，因为郑永刚意识到 ， “ 一旦市场放开，中国品牌自然会形成一个梯队式品牌市场，杉杉西服想一直独领风骚，长期成为国人的国服的可能性不大 ” 。	Just when the clothing business was in full swing, the Shanshan Group began to transform because Zheng Yonggang realized, “Once the market is liberalized, Chinese brands will naturally form an echelon brand market. Shanshan Western clothing has always dominated the style, and it is unlikely that it will become the national uniform of the Chinese people for a long time.”	yes
1999年，杉杉开始研究企业转型，郑永刚回忆当年 ， “ 我们来到上海，寻求到底转型做什么，专门找了很多专家学者，连续不断地开一些诸葛亮会、务虚研讨会。	In 1999, Shan Shan began studying enterprise transformation. Zheng Yonggang recalled that year, “We came to Shanghai to find out exactly what to do with the transformation. We specifically sought out many experts and scholars, and held continuous meetings and seminars.	yes
最后，我们设定了两个大的战略方向。	Finally, we set two major strategic directions.	yes
第一个方向是新能源新材料，另外一个是大健康有未来 ” 。	The first direction is new energy and new materials; the other is that big health has a future”.	yes
战略方向确定后，杉杉开始寻找合作，那时候鞍山热能院为鞍钢配套的炭素研究所在做国家863课题，科研经费不够，于是杉杉和鞍山热能院碳素研究所签署合作协议，共同推动国家863课题“中间相炭微球”项目产业化，从事负极材料的研发、生产和销售，在国内实现负极材料的商用推广。	After the strategic direction was determined, Shanshan began to seek cooperation. At that time, the Carbon Research Institute supporting Angang Steel of the Anshan Thermal Energy Institute was working on the national 863 project, and research funding was insufficient, so Shan Shan signed a cooperation agreement with the Anshan Thermal Energy Institute to jointly promote the industrialization of the national 863 “intermediate phase carbon microsphere” project, engage in R&D, production and sales of anode materials, and achieve commercial promotion of anode materials domestically.	yes
2001年，杉杉股份实现中间相炭微球的规模化生产，开始国产化替代，取代日本成为国内中间相炭微球主要供应商。	In 2001, Shanshan Co., Ltd. achieved large-scale production of intermediate-phase carbon microspheres and began localized replacement, replacing Japan as the main domestic supplier of intermediate-phase carbon microspheres.	no

随着锂电池的应用迅速普及，杉杉股份的锂电池业务开始逐步发展，2007年锂电材料业务被写入了杉杉股份的主营业务，服装业务营收占比逐年减少，直至2013年，杉杉股份的锂电材料业务收入全面超过服装业务。	With the rapid spread of the application of lithium batteries, the lithium battery business of Shanshan Co., Ltd. began to gradually develop. Until 2013, Shanshan Co., Ltd.'s lithium battery materials business revenue completely surpassed the clothing business.	no

The technical content in this field is relatively high. Sugisan's main competitors are the world's top 500 competitors, such as South Korea's Samsung, Japan's Sumitomo Chemical, and Nitto Denko.	no

因为大家都会去考虑，我花了那么多钱，我得去派人管对吧，这是通常会做的一个行为 ” ， 然而郑永刚则不同，杉杉收购成功的那一天，郑永刚就到杉金光电当众宣布，杉杉作为杉金的大股东，决定实施一企两制，除了郑永刚担任董事长，杉杉企业的人不派到杉金，采取授权经营的方式，原有的分配制度、企业文化、各项管理等模式不变。	Because everyone thinks about it, I've spent so much money, so I have to send someone to manage it.” But Zheng Yonggang is different. On the day Shanshan's acquisition was successful, Zheng Yonggang went to Shanjin Optoelectronics to publicly announce that Shanshan, as Shanjin's majority shareholder, decided to implement one enterprise, two systems. Except for Zheng Yonggang as the chairman, the people of Shanshan Enterprise did not send Shanjin. The original distribution system, corporate culture, and various management models remained unchanged.	no

“基金E账户”来了：证监会授权开发 投资者名下所有基金实现归集和查询 - 经济观察网 － 专业财经新闻网站	“Fund E Account” is here: the Securities Regulatory Commission authorizes the development of all funds under investors' names to collect and search - Economic Watch － A professional financial news website	yes
经济观察网 记者 陈姗 基金购买渠道繁杂导致账户信息归集不易？	Economic Watch Network reporter Chen Shan has complicated fund purchase channels, making it difficult to collect account information?	yes
总是遗忘“小金库”？	Always forget the “little treasury”?	yes
基民的这些问题即将得到解决。	The problems of the citizens of the community are about to be solved.	yes
2月10日，证监会公告称，“基金E账户”APP在各手机应用商店上架并开展公开试运行。	On February 10, the Securities Regulatory Commission announced that the “Fund E Account” app was launched on various mobile app stores and launched a public trial run.	yes
据介绍，“基金E账户”为个人投资者提供公募基金账户及份额信息的“一站式”查询服务，旨在解决广大中小投资者遗忘账户、查询繁琐等行业服务痛点。	According to the introduction, “Fund E Account” provides individual investors with a “one-stop” inquiry service for public fund account and share information. The aim is to solve industry service pain points such as the vast majority of small to medium investors forgetting accounts and making complicated inquiries.	yes
据Wind数据显示，截至2022年底，国内共有公募基金管理人156家，管理基金规模约26万亿元；公募基金份额登记机构167家，公募基金销售机构411家。	According to Wind data, by the end of 2022, there were 156 public fund managers in China, with a fund management scale of about 26 trillion yuan; 167 public fund share registration agencies and 411 public fund sales agencies.	yes
各份额登记机构账户体系相互独立，缺乏行业统一的查询渠道。	The account systems of each share registration agency are independent of each other, and there is no unified search channel for the industry.	yes
有行业人士表示，2021年末我国基金投资者超过7.2亿人，也就是说，全国有一半人都投资了基金产品。	Some people in the industry said that at the end of 2021, there were more than 720 million fund investors in China. In other words, half of the people in the country invested in fund products.	yes
此前，投资者需要通过不同销售机构查询购买情况，而通过“基金E账户”可以查询所有销售渠道购买的情况，持有基金情况一目了然。	Previously, investors needed to check the purchase situation through different sales agencies, but they could check the purchase situation through all sales channels through the “Fund E Account”, so the status of fund holdings was clear at a glance.	yes
“基金E账户”APP是什么？	What is the “Fund E Account” app?	no
据相关文件介绍，“基金E账户”APP 是中国结算经中国证监会批准开发建设的公募基金行业门户手机应用，可为投资者提供全市场公募基金产品场外份额持有情况的一站式查询。	According to relevant documents, the “Fund E Account” app is a public fund industry portal mobile application developed and built by China Settlement with the approval of the China Securities Regulatory Commission. It can provide investors with a one-stop inquiry on OTC share holdings of public fund products throughout the market.	no
投资者可以通过“基金E账户”方便、快捷地掌握自己通过全市场各销售渠道购买的各基金管理人旗下公募基金产品场外份额的持有情况，全面提升查询效率。	Through the “Fund E Account”, investors can easily and quickly grasp the OTC share of public fund products owned by various fund managers purchased through various sales channels throughout the market, improving overall inquiry efficiency.	no
具体来说，投资者可以通过“基金E账户”查询到的信息包括：在全市场各公募基金管理人处开立的基金账户信息、在公募基金销售机构处开立的交易账户信息以及持有的包括公开募集证券投资基金以及证券公司设立管理的投资者人数不受200人限制的集合资产管理计划等产品的场外份额持有情况。	Specifically, information that investors can find through “fund E accounts” includes fund account information opened by various public fund managers throughout the market, transaction account information opened by public fund sales agencies, and OTC share holdings of products including publicly raised securities investment funds and pooled asset management plans where the number of investors established and managed by securities companies is not limited to 200 people.	no
上海证券基金评价研究中心业务负责人刘亦千向经济观察网记者表示，投资者可以通过“基金E账户”App一站式获知其所有的场外公募基金持有情况，帮助其找回“被遗忘的资产”，更重要的是为客户实现了综合基金投资情况的全账户信息归集，帮助客户更及时、准确、完整的掌握自身投资情况，从而更好地优化自身的基金组合配置，更好地规划自身的财务安排。	Liu Yiqian, head of business at the Shanghai Securities Fund Evaluation Research Center, told the reporter of the Economic Watch Network that investors can use the “Fund E Account” app to know all of their OTC public fund holdings in one stop to help them recover “forgotten assets”. More importantly, it has collected full account information on the investment status of comprehensive funds for customers, helping customers to better grasp their investment situation in a timely, accurate and complete manner, so as to better optimize their own fund portfolio allocations and better plan their own financial arrangements.	no
如何注册使用？	How do I sign up for use?	no
记者注意到，目前，“基金E账户”APP已在华为、苹果、小米、OPPO、vivo等手机应用商店上架，但APP尚处于公开试运行阶段，注册需要填写邀请码，投资者可以联系所持有基金的基金管理人获取。	The reporter noticed that currently, the “Fund E Account” app has been launched on mobile app stores such as Huawei, Apple, Xiaomi, OPPO, and vivo, but the app is still in the public trial stage. Registration requires filling in an invitation code. Investors can obtain it by contacting the fund manager of the fund they hold.	no
上海一家中大型公募基金客服人员向经济观察网记者提供了一个6位数的邀请码，并告诉记者，“APP试运行阶段，中国结算提供给每个基金管理人一定数量的邀请码，投资者电话过来获取，我们都会提供。	The customer service staff of a medium to large public fund in Shanghai provided a 6-digit invitation code to the reporter of the Economic Watch Network and told the reporter, “During the trial operation of the app, China Settlement provided each fund manager with a certain number of invitation codes. Investors called to obtain them, and we would all provide them.	no
等试运行结束后，开放用户注册时就不用邀请码了。	Once the trial run is over, there is no need for an invitation code to open user registration.	no
”	”	no
记者根据证监会官网公示的“基金E账户”下载及使用说明相关文件进行了账户注册并完成查询，整个过程耗时仅几分钟，主要分为四步：用户注册、实名认证、基金账户绑定、公募基金查询。	The reporter registered the account and completed the inquiry according to the relevant documents of the “Fund E Account” download and usage instructions published on the official website of the Securities Regulatory Commission. The entire process only took a few minutes. It was mainly divided into four steps: user registration, real-name authentication, fund account binding, and public fund inquiries.	no
通过实名认证这一步之后，点击“资产”基金绑定按钮，记者通过各个基金销售平台购买的所有基金产品都呈现在绑定选项列表中（可绑定账户），完成绑定后就可以直观看到所投基金总资产并可以开始使用查询功能了。	After passing the real-name authentication step, click the “Asset” fund binding button. All fund products purchased by the reporter through various fund sales platforms are displayed in the binding options list (can be bound to accounts). After completing the binding, you can visually see the total assets of the invested funds and start using the search function.	no
值得注意的是，“基金E账户”仅为投资者提供查询服务，并不能进行申赎买卖。	It is worth noting that the “Fund E Account” only provides inquiry services for investors, and cannot conduct redemption transactions.	no
“基金 E 账户”所显示的数据日期一般为用户进行查询的日期（T日)往前推三个交易日。	The data date displayed on the “Fund E Account” is generally pushed forward three trading days from the date the user made an inquiry (T-day).	no
比如，在2 月10日打开“基金E账户”，资产页所显示的总资产、基金份额、基金净值对应日期为该日期往前推三个交易日，即2月7日。	For example, if you open a “Fund E Account” on February 10, the dates corresponding to total assets, fund shares, and fund net worth displayed on the asset page are pushed forward three trading days from that date, that is, February 7.	no

阿拉斯加上空被击落的 “物体”究竟是什么？	What exactly is the “object” that was shot down over Alaska?	yes
扑朔迷离，猜测纷纷	Confused and speculated	yes
美国军方周五（2月10日）下午再次动用美国最先进的隐身喷气战机F-22击落了一个在美国阿拉斯加上空飞行的尚未确定身份的物体。	On Friday afternoon (2/10), the US military once again used America's most advanced stealth fighter F-22 to shoot down an unidentified object flying over Alaska in the US.	yes
击落的地点距离阿拉斯加海岸十英里。	The shooting site was ten miles off the Alaskan coast.	yes
这是美军在不到一周的时间里第二次击落空中飞行物体。	This is the second time in less than a week that the US military has shot down a flying object in the air.	yes
上周六，来自中国的一个间谍气球在美国领空上漂移数日后在美国南卡罗莱纳州沿岸附近上空被击毁。	On Saturday, a spy balloon from China drifted over US airspace for a few days before being destroyed over the US coast of South Carolina.	yes
五角大楼说，第二个被击落的物体于周四晚上首次进入美国领空，在阿拉斯加东北部上空移动时被美国军方跟踪，飞行高度为1.2万米（4万英尺），其大小与一辆小型汽车差不多，与先前被击落的那个中国间谍气球相比要小很多。	The Pentagon said the second object that was shot down first entered US airspace on Thursday night and was tracked by the US military as it moved over northeastern Alaska. It flew at an altitude of 12,000 meters (40,000 feet). It was about the size of a small car, much smaller than the Chinese spy balloon that had been shot down previously.	yes
五角大楼还认为，目前没有迹象显示，这个物体是可操纵的。	The Pentagon also believes that there is currently no indication that this object can be manipulated.	yes
白宫国家安全委员会战略沟通协调员约翰·科比周五表示，虽然这个在高空飞行的物体的具体样子尚不清楚，但它“对民航飞机的安全构成了合理的威胁”。	White House National Security Council strategic communications coordinator John Bryant said on Friday that although the exact appearance of this high-altitude object is unclear, it “poses a reasonable threat to the safety of civil aviation aircraft.”	yes
科比表示，这个物体与美国境内发现的那个间谍气球不同，它上面没有悬挂“有效载荷”。	Bryant said that unlike the spy balloon discovered in the US, there was no “payload” suspended on it.	yes
科比说，“我们把它称为一个‘物体’是我们目前能够作出的最好的描述”。	Bryant said, “We call it an 'object' the best description we can make right now.”	no
拜登总统在下令击落这个物体之前听取了五角大楼的建议，他作出这个决定的时候“非常谨慎”，科比补充说。	President Biden listened to the Pentagon's advice before ordering the object to be shot down. He was “very careful” in making this decision, Bryant added.	no
美国官方对这个物体的描述大致可以归纳为：大小相当于一辆小汽车，没有操纵杆，没有悬挂装置，飞行高度为一万米左右。	The US official description of this object can be roughly summed up as the size of a small car, with no joystick, no suspension, and a flight altitude of about 10,000 meters.	no
但这些信息还无法回答基本问题，比如这个物体究竟是什么东西，它属于哪个国家，它在执行什么任务。	However, this information cannot answer basic questions, such as what kind of thing this object actually is, what country it belongs to, and what mission it is carrying out.	no
目前网上许多的分析和猜测认为，这可能又是一只中国气球。	Currently, many online analyses and speculations suggest that this may be another Chinese balloon.	no
它可能与入侵美国领空的那只间谍气球和在拉美上空飘动的那只中国气球一样都来自中国，它们在不同地点执行某种任务。	It probably came from China just like the spy balloon that invaded US airspace and the Chinese balloon that floated over Latin America; they carried out some kind of mission at different locations.	no
也有人把阿拉斯加的这个“物体”与“不明飞行物”（UFO）联系在一起。	There are also people who have linked this “object” in Alaska to a “UFO” (UFO).	no
